# Changelog

All notable changes to the Dev Process Toolkit plugin are documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.1.0/), and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).

> **Update discipline:** this file must be updated on every version bump. See the Release Checklist in `CLAUDE.md` for the required steps.

## [2.49.0] — 2026-07-17 — "Passage"

### Added
- `/upgrade` skill + version-ordered consumer-artifact migration registry with four seed script entries — M104 legacy state, v1-era orphans, stale v2.21 hooks, and permission shapes (STE-391)
- Assisted monolith-split migration entry: status-aware split of monolithic specs into the per-FR layout, with a mandatory backup and a byte-for-byte freeze of shipped history (STE-392)
- Declared + gated migration coverage: a plan-level `migration:` declaration, a `/ship-milestone` pre-flight, and gate probe #68 `migration_coverage` (STE-393)

Total test count at release: 4726 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.48.1] — 2026-07-16 — "Errata"

Docs-drift sweep (M107): the shipped docs catch up with three milestones of branch-automation changes. The template’s trunk-OK comment now names only `ci`, the placeholder docs stop calling `{type}` LLM-inferred (deterministic via `branchTypeFor` since STE-381), the technical spec’s Schema L note names the single canonical seeded default `{type}/m{N}-{slug}` (STE-388), and all five standing probe-#37 tree-leaf advisories in the technical spec are cleared — with a doc-conformance meta-test pinning every correction so the retired phrasings cannot return.

### Fixed

- Three stale branch-automation phrasings retired and five probe-#37 tree-leaf advisories cleared: `templates/CLAUDE.md.template`’s trunk-OK comment names `ci` as the only trunk-permitted type; `docs/setup-tracker-mode.md` + `docs/patterns.md` describe `{type}` as deterministically derived via `branchTypeFor` from `changelog_category` (unknown-clamp kept, `{slug}` stays LLM-inferred); `specs/technical-spec.md`’s Schema L bullet names the single canonical seeded default in every mode; the three genuinely stale tree leaves resolve again (`agents/` directory leaf, plugin-anchored layout-reference path, `<topic>` placeholder) and the two illustrative example fences use angle-bracket placeholders the probe cannot mistake for paths. One doc-conformance meta-test (15 tests) pins presence + absence per site, and a dogfood assertion holds `runCrossCuttingSpecStaleFileRefsProbe` at zero violations on this repo — probe #37 is now a de-facto error here. (STE-390)

Total test count at release: 4447 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.48.0] — 2026-07-16 — "Eponym"

Milestone-keyed branch naming (M106): the toolkit's branches now name the unit that actually ships — the milestone. One canonical branch template — `{type}/m{N}-{slug}` — replaces the deliberate-but-inconsistent mode split across every branch-creating surface (`/spec-write`'s § 7a pre-commit gate, `/implement`'s 0.b″ proposal, `/setup`'s seeded defaults), with ticket-keyed naming surviving only as a milestone-less fallback and as legacy acceptance so existing branches never re-prompt. Riding along, `/pr` sheds the one argument it never honored: PR titles are now always derived from the dominant commit's Conventional Commits subject, and free text after `/pr` gets an explicit redirect instead of silence.

### Changed

- One canonical branch template `{type}/m{N}-{slug}` everywhere: new pure selector `canonicalBranchTemplate({ milestone })` in `adapters/_shared/src/branch_proposal.ts` (m-form for a milestone-bound FR, `{type}/{ticket-id}-{slug}` fallback otherwise) drives `/spec-write`'s § 7a gate and `/implement`'s 0.b″ proposal with `{N}` resolved from the FR's `milestone:` frontmatter; an explicit Schema L `branch_template:` value still wins and the absent-key skip is unchanged. FR-scoped acceptability is re-keyed — `RunScope` gains optional `milestoneNumber`, acceptable IFF off-trunk AND (word-bounded `m<N>` match OR legacy tracker-ID / short-ULID substring), word-boundary corpus extended (`m105` ≠ `m1051`) — so both naming generations pass without re-prompting. `/setup` step 7c seeds the single default in BOTH tracker mode and `mode: none`, `/setup --migrate` re-seeds only a value byte-identical to the retired seeded default (logged in `## /setup audit`; custom values untouched, absent stays absent, helper `reseedBranchTemplate`), and the four shipped docs no longer present the ticket-keyed form as a seeded default. (STE-388)

### Removed

- `/pr`'s `[PR title]` positional argument — the frontmatter `argument-hint` and the buried "use it" `$ARGUMENTS` Notes bullet are gone; the Step-5 Title bullet is hardened to derived-only (always the dominant commit's Conventional Commits subject, no user-supplied override path) and a Notes rule pins the exact redirect — "PR titles are derived from the commit subject; amend the commit to change the title" — for free text after `/pr`. README's Commands table renders the `/pr` Args cell as `—` with the new "— marks a skill that takes no arguments" note, `specs/testing-spec.md`'s Tier-1 frontmatter row is conditional ("argument-hint where the skill takes arguments") so a hint-less `/pr` conforms, and one doc-conformance meta-test pins every removal. (STE-389)

Total test count at release: 4432 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.47.0] — 2026-07-16 — "Synopsis"

FR Summary section + review contract (M105): the toolkit's first external-user feedback (GitHub issue #39, "specs are too detailed to review") ships additively — every FR `/spec-write` creates now opens with a plain-language `## Summary` written for human reviewers, a new gate-check probe holds that summary to a deterministic altitude rule, and the review contract is stated at every approval touchpoint: the human approves Summary + Requirement + Acceptance Criteria, while Technical Design + Testing are implementation-facing, verified by the deterministic gates and the TDD audit. No existing section loses precision; no existing FR is edited.

### Added

- `/spec-write` § 0b authors `## Summary` as the first FR body section on every new-FR create — 3–6 non-empty lines of plain prose under an altitude rule (zero backticks, no AC-ID tokens, no path-like tokens), included in the step 4 draft-gate preview and seeded naturally from `/brainstorm`'s approved-decision recap. `docs/layout-reference.md`'s FR-section contract names `## Summary` a third sanctioned optional section (first-in-body), probe #40's remedy names it optional instead of claiming a closed 5-section shape, and tracker-ride fixtures prove the Linear AC-sync normalize path is byte-blind to a leading Summary while the unchanged `ticket_description_template` opens every ticket description with it — zero adapter code changes. (STE-385)
- Gate-check probe #67 `fr_summary_altitude` (severity error): a new shared scanner enforces the four altitude rules over `## Summary` sections of active FRs only — closed rule-id set `line_cap` / `backtick` / `ac_id` / `path_token`, with `ac_id` matching every AC-ID flavor (tracker-mode and mode-none short-ULID alike) and the section bound at the next level-2 heading so an h3 subheading can never mask later violations — and is byte-identically vacuous when the section is absent, so pre-M105, tracker-imported, and hand-authored FRs never turn red. README probe pins move 66 → 67 with the count-drift meta-test regexes in the same commit; a dogfood assertion runs the scanner over this repo's own active FRs. (STE-386)
- The review contract — "the human approves the Summary, Requirement, and Acceptance Criteria; Technical Design and Testing are implementation-facing and are verified by the deterministic gates and the TDD audit" — is stated at the `/spec-write` draft gate, § 4 review-and-confirm, and the Rules draft-approval rule, in `docs/sdd-methodology.md` (new "Spec-Time Review Is Scoped" lifecycle entry) and `docs/workflow-overview.md`'s gate table, and as a reviewer-facing bullet in the consumer CLAUDE.md template — generalizing the `--no-tech` split from optional deferral to stated default, token-free at every site. (STE-387)

Total test count at release: 4368 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.46.0] — 2026-07-16 — "Homestead"

`.dpt` layout consolidation (M104): the toolkit's two root-level state folders — `.dpt-locks/` (tracked lock coordination) and `.dev-process/` (git-ignored token ledger) — collapse into one `.dpt/` tree that preserves their opposite VCS semantics: `.dpt/locks/` stays tracked, `.dpt/ledger/` + `.dpt/scratch/` are ignored via a committed `.dpt/.gitignore` the toolkit writes and owns. A new `dpt_paths.ts` is the single source of every `.dpt` path literal, and the relayout fixes two latent defects it exposed — a hard-coded lock-scan pathspec that would have silently double-claimed after the move, and a file/directory namespace collision that threw `EISDIR` — both dissolved structurally rather than papered over with a guard. A dot-anchored path-drift meta-test locks the retired literals out for good.

### Changed

- Consolidate `.dpt-locks/` + `.dev-process/` into one `.dpt/` tree governed by `adapters/_shared/src/dpt_paths.ts`, the sole composer of `.dpt` path literals (`dptRoot` / `locksDir` / `ledgerPath` / `scratchDir` / `scratchRoot`; pure path composition, no I/O). `LocalProvider.findRemoteBranchWithLock` now derives its `ls-tree` pathspec from `this.locksDir` (repo-root-relative via `relative`) instead of a hard-coded `.dpt-locks/${id}` literal — closing a latent double-claim after the move — and the file/directory `EISDIR` namespace collision is dissolved by separating tracked locks (`.dpt/locks/`) from ignored scratch (`.dpt/scratch/`) with no defensive guard added. Gate-check probes #41/#64 re-point to `.dpt/scratch/**` with vacuity preserved; the token ledger moves to `.dpt/ledger/`. (STE-382)
- `/setup` writes a committed, self-contained `.dpt/.gitignore` (`ledger/` + `scratch/`, deliberately relative so it is position-independent) via the idempotent byte-compare `writeDptGitignore` helper, replacing the retired `.dev-process/` append to the consumer's root `.gitignore` (AC-STE-344.5). The toolkit's own root `.gitignore` gains **no** `.dpt/` line — a blanket root entry would defeat the nested file, since git never descends into an excluded directory — and the legacy `.dev-process/` directory is deleted forward-only. Docs describe the tree, the tracked/ignored split, and the accepted blanket-root hazard. (STE-383)

### Added

- `tests/dpt-path-drift.test.ts` — a grep meta-test (STE-49 shape) that fails naming `file:line` if a retired `.dpt-locks` / `.dev-process` literal reappears under `docs/`, `skills/`, `adapters/`, `templates/`, `README.md`, or the cross-cutting specs. The `.dev-process` pattern is dot-anchored so it never matches `dev-process-toolkit`, the plugin's own name; `*.test.ts` decoy files and history surfaces (`CHANGELOG.md`, `specs/**/archive/`) are exempt with commented rationale, and tripwire fixtures prove the gate actually fires. (STE-384)

Total test count at release: 4318 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.45.0] — 2026-07-15 — "Signpost"

Spec-write flow determinism (M103): the `/spec-write` closing `Next:` line now points milestone-bound work at the milestone close — the variant rule is re-keyed from new-FR presence to **milestone binding**, guarded by new doc-shape probe #66 — and kickoff branch types become a pure function of FR frontmatter: `changelog_category`-keyed `branchTypeFor` replaces the freestyle LLM `{type}` pass, so identically-shaped FRs propose identically-typed branches every session.

### Changed

- `/spec-write` `Next:`-line variant rule re-keyed on **milestone binding**: a run that writes ≥ 1 milestone-bound FR recommends `/dev-process-toolkit:implement M<N>` (one `Next:` line per distinct milestone), milestone-less FRs keep the FR-id form, and the retired new-FR-presence discriminator sentence is deleted. The rule paragraph, both tail-template `Next:` lines, and the retired-sentence absence tripwire are pinned by gate-check probe #66 (`runSpecWriteNextLineDocProbe`; README probe count 65 → 66); `/implement`'s § Invocation forms lede drops the "`/spec-write`'s next step" claim. (STE-380)
- Deterministic branch-type derivation: pure `branchTypeFor({ changelogCategory, noTech })` (`--no-tech` ⇒ `chore`; `Fixed`/`Security` ⇒ `fix`; else `feat`) feeds both `buildBranchProposal` consumers (`/spec-write` § 7a and `/implement` 0.b″ — the LLM pass is rescoped to `{slug}` only), and `buildFRFrontmatter` gains a `changelogCategory` opt so every new FR carries an explicit `changelog_category:` line. (STE-381)

### Fixed

- `shipped_in: null` template sentinel handling: `plan_ship_coherence` now classifies the pre-ship sentinel as unshipped debt instead of a corrupt stamp (keeping `bun test` green during the archive-then-ship transient), and `stampShippedIn` overwrites the sentinel in place as the first real stamp instead of refusing as a double-ship. (mid-ceremony fix, no FR)

Total test count at release: 4181 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.44.0] — 2026-07-10 — "Consent"

Token-stats opt-in (M102): the per-skill token accounting introduced in M92 is now opt-in and **off by default**. A dedicated, always-emitted `## Token Stats` section in `CLAUDE.md` (closed key set `{enabled}`, default `false`) gates the feature end-to-end — when disabled, the bundled `SessionEnd`/`Stop` capture hook reads the flag and no-ops (no ledger writes; fail-off **and** fail-open, so a malformed or absent config never blocks session teardown), and all three render sites emit nothing. Existing projects stay off until they re-run `/setup`, for free via the `absent-section ⇒ off` parser convention. `/spec-write` now reports an honest `token_stats_disabled` disposition instead of falsely claiming a render. This repo dogfoods `enabled: true`, so the toolkit keeps accounting its own usage.

### Changed

- Token Stats opt-in config surface: an always-emitted `## Token Stats` `CLAUDE.md` section (closed `{enabled}` key set, default `false`), a `readTokenStatsConfig` parser mirroring `readVerificationConfig` (missing file or section ⇒ off), a one-at-a-time `/setup` interview step + a `## /setup audit` row, and documentation in `docs/layout-reference.md`. (STE-378)
- Token Stats enforcement: the bundled `session-token-ledger.ts` capture hook and all three `## Token Stats` render sites (`/spec-write`, `/implement` archival, `/ship-milestone` rollup) now gate on the flag — capture no-ops when disabled (fail-off + fail-open, never throwing at session-end) and `/spec-write` emits the `token_stats_disabled` XOR `token_stats_rendered` disposition (new capability key; canonical set 30 → 31). (STE-379)

Total test count at release: 4100 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.43.0] — 2026-07-09 — "Attested"

Fork-consumer reliability (M100): a scary-looking fork output no longer cascades into silent feature-death or a false high-severity alarm. Closes the `deps-research` fork enforcement asymmetry (the deterministic gate its `spec-research` twin already had) and makes `/report-issue` evidence-based — capturing the session that actually contains the incident and refusing to assert high severity without evidence. Origin: a 2026-07-09 `/report-issue` gist reporting a deps-research prompt-injection whose own attached transcript neither reproduced nor even invoked the fork.

### Added

- Deps-research fork enforcement parity: the deterministic `deps_research_result_shape` gate (#64) — a structural clone of the `spec-research` twin's #41 probe, reusing the `parseDepsResearchBlock` parser — plus a definition-level `deps_research_disposition_contract` gate (#65). Two no-silent-skip disposition tokens (`deps_research_skipped_no_manifest` / `_no_tech`) make the complete legal disposition set byte-checkable, with no legal token for "compromised"/"injected"/"disabled", and an anti-cascade rule forbids the cross-invocation "fork compromised" belief that caused the original incident. Retires the now-obsolete STE-318 A14 phantom-probe guard (the probe is real now). (STE-373)
- `/report-issue` evidence gate: marker-matched incident-session selection (`selectIncidentSession`) over the K most-recent candidate transcripts with the most-recent-mtime pick as fallback — fixing wrong-session capture — plus a pre-publish evidence check (`verifyIncidentEvidence`) and an advisory, never-blocking severity cap that tags a `high`/`critical` report whose incident is absent from its own captured transcript (`verified: false` + a `verification` block in `metadata.json`). (STE-374)

Total test count at release: 4059 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.42.0] — 2026-07-07 — "Tally"

Per-skill token-usage stats (M92): the toolkit now records what each SDD skill costs. A fail-open hook captures per-(skill, model) token aggregates from the session transcript into a git-ignored ledger, and machine-managed `## Token Stats` blocks project it into spec files only at moments a spec file is already being written/committed — never a standalone dirty-tree event. A deliberate, measurement-only reversal of the prior "no token counts" stance (no caps introduced).

### Added

- Token-usage capture layer: `parseTranscriptTokenUsage` groups every transcript line's `message.usage` by `(attributionSkill ?? "(main-loop)", model)` — `context:fork` children roll up into their parent skill for free — and a `SessionEnd`/`Stop` bundled hook writes the session's rows to the git-ignored `.dev-process/token-ledger.jsonl` (idempotent per `session_id`, fail-open exit 0, self-healing on corrupted lines, atomic temp-file + rename writes). `.gitignore` wiring lands here and as `/setup` step 6c. (STE-344)
- `## Token Stats` FR block: sentinel-fenced, machine-managed, placed last (after `## Notes`), byte-stable per-skill × per-model table with separate `brainstorm`/`spec-write` rows + subtotal; idempotent `upsertTokenStatsBlock` replace-in-place; convention test + FR-section-contract tolerance note; `/spec-write` renders it riding its own FR-file write and emits the `token_stats_rendered` capability row; brainstorm→FR bridging claims the most-recent unclaimed same-branch brainstorm session with durable `claimed_by` persistence (`claimRowsForFR`) so no FR double-counts. (STE-345)
- Commit-boundary renders: `/implement` Phase 4 re-renders each in-scope FR's block into the archive commit (after `git mv`/flip, before commit), and `/ship-milestone` renders a milestone rollup into `specs/plan/M<N>.md` inside the release commit — per-FR subtotals, `(main-loop)`, a `design/exploration` bucket for never-claimed brainstorm rows, and a per-model `total`; idempotent + non-interfering, proven by test. (STE-346)

Total test count at release: 3988 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.41.0] — 2026-07-06 — "Labeled"

Closes the milestone-label coverage holes (M97) found on a downstream Jira project, where an FR-backed ticket shipped without its `milestone-M5` label and the gap went permanently invisible the moment its FR archived. Enforcement is FR-backed-only by design — bugs and ad-hoc tickets are never milestone-scoped.

### Added

- Archival-boundary milestone-binding assertion: `assertMilestoneBindingAtArchive` runs per FR before any `git mv` at `/spec-archive` and `/implement` Phase-4-close — adapter-aware (Linear `projectMilestone.name` byte-equality / Jira `milestone-<M-token>` label), attempt-then-refuse (one retrying attach, NFR-10 refusal on still-missing, the milestone-group batch skips only the offender), and never throws (a dead ticket fetch converts to a refusal with cause). Emits `milestone_label_asserted_at_archive` / `milestone_label_archive_refused` per archived FR. (STE-363)
- `/spec-archive --backfill-milestone-labels`: one-shot remediation sweep over active + archived FRs — fetches each bound ticket and attaches any missing milestone binding. Dry-run by default, `--apply` to write, idempotent, best-effort per ticket with a `backfilled`/`already-correct`/`failed` aggregate report naming each failed ticket and its plan file. (STE-364)

### Fixed

- Milestone attach is reliable at write time: the attach + read-back-verify round-trip retries transient failures on the canonical `1s+2s+4s` schedule (a binding-mismatch `MilestoneAttachmentError` never retries; the success path adds no latency), the § 0.e attach + verify is guaranteed per FR on every `/implement` path including the milestone-scope fan-out, and a permanent failure surfaces as the loud `milestone_attach_failed` capability row (severity ≥ warning) instead of a silent info line. (STE-362)

Total test count at release: 3898 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.40.0] — 2026-07-06 — "Stamped"

Makes "shipped" a deterministic file property and turns the post-merge ship ceremony from unsupported folklore into a guided, gate-backed flow (M99) — motivated by M98 sitting merged-but-unshipped for two days with every version signal coherently stale.

### Added

- `/ship-milestone` stamps `shipped_in: v<X.Y.Z>` into the resolved plan's frontmatter inside the atomic release commit (live and archive-fallback paths); `stampShippedIn` helper is byte-preserving, idempotent, and double-ship-guarded; a one-shot backfill stamped all 95 legacy archived plans. (STE-368)
- `plan_ship_coherence` gate probe (#63, ERROR): stamped archived plans must match a CHANGELOG heading, archived-unstamped-unparked fails the gate with the ceremony-recipe remedy, and `ship_state: parked` renders as a GATE PASSED WITH NOTES row; `/spec-archive` gains `--parked` + both exit hints. (STE-369)
- Post-merge ceremony surfacing: `/pr` soft ship-state pre-flight (`[m]erge later / [s]hip first / [a]bort` + `Follow-up:` PR-body line), bare-`/ship-milestone` ship-debt offer, opt-in `Open ceremony PR via /pr now?` chain after off-trunk release commits, and a `## Post-merge ceremony` recipe in the reference docs. (STE-370)

Total test count at release: 3819 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.39.0] — 2026-07-06 — "Headless"

Hardens the autonomous headless (`claude -p`) `/conformance-loop` path (M98) — fixes the three smoke/conformance infrastructure findings from the 2026-07-04 live run so an autonomous run gets past its own driver and actually exercises the plugin under test.

### Changed

- Workspace trust becomes an operator **precondition** instead of a self-write. `/smoke-test` asserts `hasTrustDialogAccepted` (never writes it — the harness self-modification classifier denies that write under `claude -p`) and refuses with the jq seed one-liner if absent; `/conformance-loop` gains an up-front pre-flight (h) asserting both test-project paths; teardown no longer removes trust (operator-owned, persistent). Supersedes STE-356's self-seed. (STE-367)

### Fixed

- Fire-and-exit guard: `/smoke-test` Phase 2 opens with a `SMOKE-CTX` `[ -t 0 ]` context probe so the driver can no longer misidentify its `claude -p` context as interactive, plus a co-located prohibition on `run_in_background` / `Monitor` / turn-yield at both drivers' spawn sites and a drift meta-test. Attacks the F3 root cause that recurred despite M96's prose guardrails. (STE-365)
- zsh-safe glob fences: the Phase 0.5 wipe `rm` + verify `ls` are wrapped in `bash -c` (preserving the STE-358 fence shape) and the final-message self-check `for`-loops are `nullglob`-guarded, so an unmatched glob no longer aborts under zsh's default `nomatch` — which had false-PASSed the verified wipe. (STE-366)

Total test count at release: 3762 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.38.0] — 2026-07-04 — "Test Drive"

Gives toolkit users a place to plug in a post-`/implement` "does it actually run / look right?" check — because a green gate has never proven the app boots. A `## Verification` convention declares a project's check skill; a new `/implement` Phase 4b″ hook discovers and runs it after the gate passes, reports the outcome advisorily, and on failure classifies spec-gap vs impl-bug and proposes the next command (never auto-invoking it). `/setup` and `/implement` scaffold a stack-aware "drive" stub, or fall back to the generic `/visual-check` for small web UIs. Offers default to decline in non-interactive runs so an autonomous `/implement` never stalls.

### Added

- **STE-347 — `## Verification` convention + `/implement` Phase 4b″ hook.** A closed `{verify_skill, verify_mode}` CLAUDE.md block (`verify_mode ∈ {advisory (default), blocking, manual}`) plus a shared discovery-precedence resolver (declared → scan `.claude/skills/*` candidates → adopt-offer → ambiguity-ask → none) and a Phase 4b″ hook that runs the resolved check after gate-GREEN and before the step-14 report, gates the commit under `blocking`, and emits one of six literal `verify_skill_*` capability tokens. (STE-347)
- **STE-348 — Stack-aware check-skill generator + scaffold-if-missing + `/visual-check` fallback.** A collision-safe `scaffoldCheckSkill` helper (slug charset-validated) shared by `/setup`'s opt-in seed step and `/implement`'s no-check branch writes a runnable `.claude/skills/<slug>-drive/SKILL.md` stub from four stack templates (Flutter / web / Python / generic), each carrying `disable-model-invocation: true`; `verify_skill: visual-check` is a valid zero-authoring value that routes Phase 4b″ to the shipped `/visual-check`. (STE-348)
- **STE-349 — Verification-skills docs, `patterns.md` entry, and per-stack examples.** A new `docs/verification-skills.md` authoring guide, a `patterns.md` "Project-Authored Verification Skills" pattern cross-linking the Visual-Verification and Verification-Before-Completion patterns, worked check-skill examples for TypeScript/web, Flutter, and Python, and README + methodology cross-links. (STE-349)

Total test count at release: 3739 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.37.0] — 2026-07-03 — "Patience"

Teaches both smoke drivers to actually wait: the fire-and-exit WAIT step becomes a bounded multi-iteration poll, the Phase 0.5 wipe is verified on disk with freshness-gated chain-completeness checks so stale logs can't false-pass, orphaned grandchildren are adopted instead of abandoned, and two plugin-side fixes let /setup's placeholder ride its own bootstrap commit and document the team-managed Jira status-vocabulary path.

### Added

- **STE-357 — Enforce the wait discipline: bounded multi-iteration polls, no turn-end with live pidfiles.** Both driver poll fences become bounded `for i in $(seq 1 18); do kill -0 … || break; sleep 30; done` loops (≈9 min per call, `kill -0` first so the harness leading-sleep block can't reject them); red-flag prose names the harness sleep-block hint recommending `run_in_background`/Monitor as NOT-license — background-wait + end-turn IS the fire-and-exit failure; a final-message self-check re-runs the pidfile-liveness fence and resumes polling while any pidfile is live. Runtime validation ships `[~]` pending the next conformance run. (STE-357)
- **STE-358 — Verified Phase 0.5 wipe + freshness-gated chain-completeness checks.** The wipe widens to every per-run scratch class (prompt/`.log`/`.pid`/`.rc`/`.start`/`.attempt*`/mcp-config) with a post-`rm` `ls` zero-survivors assertion replacing self-report (survivors ⇒ NFR-10 refusal naming them); `assertChainIntegrity` gains an optional `runStart` parameter — a capture whose mtime predates run-start is `capture stale (pre-run)`, never healthy — wired into `/smoke-test` Phase 2.Y and `/conformance-loop` Phase A; Phase 1 step 6 documents that the child model layer denies all settings.json writes, so pre-creation must carry the full final allow-list. (STE-358)
- **STE-359 — Orphan adoption for surviving grandchildren.** `/conformance-loop` Phase A scans the leg's six-skill pidfiles after a driver exits and adopts any still-answering PID — polled to exit with the bounded discipline before the leg-completeness check runs (adoption recovers evidence, not the chain); both drivers document the killed-with-parent vs survives-as-orphan nondeterminism as a residual risk with adoption as the deterministic recovery. Runtime validation ships `[~]`. (STE-359)
- **STE-360 — Exempt the /setup Bun zero-match placeholder from pre-commit-tdd-orchestrator.** Staged `src/.placeholder.test.ts` carrying the `Bun zero-match workaround` marker (or staged as a deletion) no longer blocks the bootstrap commit; the dual key reads the index blob so a marker-less rename stays tdd-required, and mixed commits still require /tdd evidence; /setup's step 8b documents that the placeholder rides the bootstrap commit. (STE-360)

## [2.36.0] — 2026-07-02 — "Integrity"

Makes the smoke-driver chain complete end-to-end headless: Phase 0.5 cleanup is scoped per tracker so tandem legs can't delete each other's live MCP config, every grandchild spawn is detached + pidfile-polled past the 10-minute Bash ceiling with an end-of-run chain-integrity assertion barring truncated runs from green, and workspace trust is pre-seeded so the scaffolded allow-list actually enforces at the grandchild layer.

### Added

- **STE-354 — Scope Phase 0.5 mcp-config cleanup to the resolved tracker.** `/smoke-test` Phase 0.5 now removes only `dpt-smoke-mcp-config-<tracker>.json` — the cross-tracker glob that raced the concurrent tandem leg's Phase 1 write (2026-07-02 F1) is gone; the STE-186 staleness intent is preserved per-leg, and § Operator-driven parallelism documents the cleanup as per-tracker-scoped by the same isolation invariant. (STE-354)
- **STE-355 — Grandchild spawn lifecycle: detached spawn + bounded poll + chain-integrity assertion.** Every canonical-chain spawn (all six `/smoke-test` Phase 2 fences AND `/conformance-loop` Phase A's two legs) is now detached with PID capture and awaited via bounded `kill -0` + `sleep 30` poll calls — no single foreground Bash call caps a grandchild at the harness 600s ceiling (F2), and ending the session with a live pidfile is forbidden (F3). New `assertChainIntegrity` (exists + non-empty + stream-json `result` event per expected capture) runs as Phase 2.Y and bars truncated runs from a green summary with the pinned `STE-355 regression: chain truncated — <child> (<reason>)` diagnostic; `/conformance-loop` Phase A mirrors it with a leg-completeness check that fails an incomplete leg regardless of RC 0. (STE-355)
- **STE-356 — Pre-seed workspace trust so the scaffolded allow-list enforces.** `/smoke-test` Phase 1 step 6b seeds `projects["<path>"].hasTrustDialogAccepted` in the live `$CLAUDE_CONFIG_DIR/.claude.json` via backup + merge-only jq + atomic `mv` under a bounded cross-leg spinlock; a spawn-time gate refuses (NFR-10) when the entry is missing and logs the `workspace_trust_seeded` token when present; new `checkAllowlistInert` detector turns any captured "Ignoring … permissions.allow entries" warning into a high-severity finding; both threat models name workspace trust as an enforcement precondition, and Phase 5 removes the seeded entries + backup. (STE-356)

### Fixed

A non-zero `dart run` exit now triggers one `pub get` refresh + retry before falling back; parse/empty/not-array failures (run exited 0) still short-circuit unchanged. (STE-340)

## [2.31.1] — 2026-05-27 — "Unified"

M87 fixes the milestone-binding parser drift that silently disabled M86/STE-329's binding on every current-format plan. The write path (attach) and the verify path (`/gate-check` probe #26) each carried a private H1+em-dash-only regex, but the live plan template and `/spec-write` emit `## M<N>: <title>` (H2 + colon) — so attach threw ("no recognizable heading") and the probe skipped vacuously for every downstream consumer.

### Fixed

- **STE-335 — Unify the plan-heading parser.** New shared `parsePlanHeading` (`adapters/_shared/src/plan_heading.ts`) matches a milestone heading at `#` or `##` depth, with an em-dash or colon separator, and an optional trailing `{#M<N>}` anchor, normalizing every form to the canonical `M<N> — <title>` (em-dash). Both `planFileHeadingToMilestoneName` (`attach_project_milestone.ts`) and probe #26's `readPlanHeading` (`tracker_project_milestone_attached.ts`) delegate to it; the two duplicate `^# (M\d+ — …)` regex copies are deleted. This restores M86/STE-329's milestone binding — both the Linear `object` and Jira `label` paths — end-to-end for every project whose plans come from the current template. Probe #26's missing-binding remedy also becomes binding-aware: the Jira `label` path now points at `editJiraIssue` (read-merge-write the `milestone-<M-token>` label) instead of misdirecting to Linear's `save_issue`. (STE-335)

Total test count at release: 3257 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

The MCP exposes no version/milestone create-or-list tool, so the milestone M-number is mirrored onto each Jira issue as a create-on-write `milestone-M<N>` label via `editJiraIssue` (read-merge-write, read-back verified) instead of a Linear-style projectMilestone object. Flips the Jira adapter's long-standing `project_milestone: false` (STE-38/STE-154) to `true`, and `attachProjectMilestone` + `/gate-check` probe #26 become adapter-aware.

### Added

The shared `attachProjectMilestone` helper (`adapters/_shared/src/attach_project_milestone.ts`) gains a `label` branch: derive `milestone-<M-token>` (leading `M\d+` of the canonical plan-H1 name — labels forbid spaces, so the title never leaks), attach read-merge-write via `addLabel` (union, idempotent, never clobbering `default_labels`/operator labels), and verify by re-reading the issue's `labels`; missing/mismatched → `MilestoneAttachmentError` (now binding-aware: Jira-appropriate remedy on the label path, Linear remedy on the object path). `/gate-check` probe #26 (`tracker_project_milestone_attached.ts`) becomes adapter-aware too — the Jira branch asserts `labels` contains `milestone-<M-token>`, and the tracker-key parse was generalized from `linear:`-only to any `<key>:` so genuine `jira:`-bound FRs are found. The Linear `object` path is byte-identical (no regression). `/spec-write` § 0b, `/implement` Phase 1 step 0.e, and `docs/tracker-adapters.md` un-Linear-only the milestone-attach surface. The live-Jira smoke (AC-STE-329.9) ships `[~]` — this repo is mode:linear, so no in-repo Jira FR exercises the branch. (STE-329)

## [2.27.0] — 2026-05-18 — "Forked"

M80 codifies the canonical audit-fix loop pattern, lands a `/gate-check` probe enforcing its frontmatter invariants, migrates `/spec-review` to the pattern as the first conformance example, and removes a Flutter/Dart placeholder cruft from `/setup`. The canonical pattern (Pattern 29 in `docs/patterns.md`, stable anchor `{#pattern-audit-fix-loop}`) describes a main-context orchestrator dispatching via Skill tool into a forked child skill (`context: fork` + `agent:` + `user-invocable: false`) paired with a read-only subagent that emits findings via a fenced `<role>-result` block; the orchestrator parses, then dispatches the fix into another fork or halts. STE-225's `/tdd` four-stage orchestrator + STE-296's `tdd-spec-reviewer` audit step are the canonical precedents; HG95VF's M9 design is documented as the superseded ancestor. `/simplify` (M81+) and `/implement` Phase 3 Stage B (M82+) migrations follow in later milestones.

### Added

- **STE-306 — Audit-fix loop pattern doc.** New section "Audit-fix loop" in `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/docs/patterns.md` (Pattern 29, stable anchor `{#pattern-audit-fix-loop}`) codifies the canonical shape — main-context orchestrator → Skill tool → forked child → paired read-only subagent → fenced `<role>-result` block → orchestrator parses + dispatches fix into another fork. Classifies the four current loops in the toolkit: `/tdd` four-stage group as canonical, `/spec-review` as legacy (no fork at all — superseded by STE-308 in this milestone), `/implement` Phase 3 Stage B + `/simplify` as legacy (in-process fix). Documents the in-process-fix exception with rationale (Claude Code forbids nested subagent spawns AND the fixer needs the orchestrator's full implementation context) and the deferred M82+ migration path. Forward-link cross-refs to STE-307 (probe) and STE-308 (`/spec-review` migration); back-link cross-ref to STE-225 / STE-296 / HG95VF. `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/tdd/SKILL.md` adds a "See also" line to the new anchor. (STE-306)
- **STE-307 — Gate-check probe for audit-fix loop pattern invariants.** New `/gate-check` probe #54 `audit_fix_loop_pattern_invariants` (severity: error) at `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/adapters/_shared/src/audit_fix_loop_pattern.ts`. Const allowlist `AUDIT_FIX_LOOP_CANONICAL_LOOPS` exports audit-fork pairs (`{ orchestrator, child, subagent }`). The probe asserts (a) the paired child skill exists with `context: fork`, `user-invocable: false`, and `agent:` resolving to an existing `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/agents/<name>.md`; (b) the subagent declares `tools: Read, Grep, Glob` only (Write/Edit/Bash/Agent excluded); (c) the child's `allowed-tools:` (when present) excludes `Agent`. Reuses frontmatter-parsing primitives (`parseFrontmatterFields` / `lineNumberOfKey` / `splitToolsList` / `pushViolation`) from `tdd_probe_helpers.ts` shared with probes #39 / #50 / #51. Allowlist ships at FR ship with the `/tdd` audit-fork pair (`tdd-spec-review` / `tdd-spec-reviewer`) only — the action subagents' orchestrator-level invariants stay with probe #39 `tdd_orchestrator_integrity`. Vacuous when neither `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/` nor `agents/` is present (matches probes #39 / #50 / #51 shape). Spec deviation resolved during `/implement`: AC.2 narrowed from the original four-entry list to audit-fork-only to match the M80 plan's stated architecture ("per-skill audit fork + paired read-only subagent"). Test coverage: `tests/gate-check-audit-fix-loop-pattern-invariants.test.ts` (24 tests including a self-run sanity assertion against the dogfood repo). (STE-307)

### Changed

- **STE-308 — /spec-review forked-auditor migration.** Migrates `/spec-review` from a fully main-context audit skill to the canonical audit-fix loop pattern as the first conformance example proving the pattern works on a real skill. New read-only subagent `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/agents/spec-reviewer.md` (`tools: Read, Grep, Glob`; `model: sonnet`; `maxTurns: 8`) handles the audit task — read `specs/frs/`, scan implementation, build the traceability map, classify each AC as ✓/✗/⚠, detect drift. New paired forked child skill `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/spec-review-audit/SKILL.md` (`context: fork`, `agent: spec-reviewer`, `user-invocable: false`). New deterministic parser `parseSpecReviewResultBlock(text): SpecReviewResult` at `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/adapters/_shared/src/spec_review_result.ts` with required sections `## Traceability map` / `## Findings` / `## Drift hints` and required AC-row fields (`ac`, `impl`, `test`, `status ∈ {done|missing|partial}`); format violations name the offending field in the same shape as `parseTddSpecReviewResultBlock`. `/spec-review` SKILL.md rewritten to dispatch via `Skill('dev-process-toolkit:spec-review-audit')` and parse the returned fenced block (single bounded retry on parse failure per STE-296 mode-D pattern, then halt with NFR-10 refusal). `/spec-review` added to `AUDIT_FIX_LOOP_CANONICAL_LOOPS` allowlist (now two audit-fork pairs: `/tdd` + `/spec-review`); `spec-review-audit` added to `NON_COMMIT_PRODUCING_SKILLS` allowlist in `commit_producing_skill_branch_gate.ts`. `formatDriftHint` contract from `spec_review_drift_hint.ts` preserved unchanged (threshold ≥ 2; main computes the line emission, fork emits the count). Test coverage: `tests/spec-review-result-parser.test.ts` (19 tests) + `tests/spec-review-fork-migration.test.ts` (27 tests). (STE-308)

### Fixed

- **STE-309 — Remove Flutter/Dart `test/empty_test.dart` placeholder from `/setup`.** The `/setup` SKILL.md Flutter/Dart stack-specific guidance bullet no longer instructs writing a placeholder test file. The bullet now states explicitly that `flutter create .` writes `test/widget_test.dart` automatically, includes the literal directive "do NOT add an extra placeholder file (e.g. `test/empty_test.dart`)", and notes that flutter test exits 0 against an empty `test/` directory on current Flutter SDKs. Downstream Flutter/Dart packages carrying `test/empty_test.dart` from older `/setup` runs should delete the file manually — flutter test exits 0 on empty `test/` on current SDKs. No automated codemod, no `/gate-check` probe, no version-sniffing logic ships with this FR — documentation-only on `/setup` plus this CHANGELOG cleanup callout. Spec deviation resolved during `/implement`: AC.2 relaxed from the original "no `empty_test` substring at all" to "no `expect(1, 1)` body AND no instructed `test/*.dart` other than `test/widget_test.dart`" — the AC.1-mandated counter-example literal is permitted inside the do-NOT-add directive. Test coverage: `tests/setup-skill-flutter-no-placeholder.test.ts` (6 tests). (STE-309)

Total test count at release: 2097 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.26.0] — 2026-05-18 — "Mapped"

M79 promotes status mapping from per-adapter strict equality to a per-project YAML config with a tolerance wrapper that prompts the operator on non-key encounters instead of failing the gate. The plugin now reads `specs/tracker-config.yaml` (written by `/setup` via MCP-fetch + LLM proposal + diff-approval); a single wrapper at the Provider boundary routes `Provider.getTicketStatus` through a three-way return (mapped role / `null` known-non-key / `"unknown"` sentinel) and surfaces force/skip/cancel on non-key encounters interactively (advisory under non-tty CI). Gate probes #8 + #14 (STE-54 + STE-87 strict equality) now honor the wrapper; STE-151 carve-outs preserved verbatim. Dogfooded: this repo's own `specs/tracker-config.yaml` ships with the release.

### Added

- **STE-302 — Per-project tracker-config.yaml + status role vocabulary.** New loader module `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/adapters/_shared/src/tracker_config.ts` exposes `readTrackerConfig` / `writeTrackerConfig` / `validateTrackerConfig` / `roleToStatus` / `statusToRole` with `TrackerConfigShapeError` (NFR-10 canonical refusal shape). Canonical role enum locked at four values: `initial`, `in_progress`, `in_review`, `done`; missing role surfaces validation error. `statusToRole` returns the role name (mapped) / `null` (status in `statuses:` but unmapped — known-non-key) / `"unknown"` (status not in `statuses:` — drift). New helper `adapters/_shared/src/resolve_status_mapping.ts` is the integration chokepoint: tracker-config → adapter frontmatter → inline fallback. New `/gate-check` probe #52 `tracker_config_shape` (severity: error) byte-checks schema invariants. Test coverage: `tests/tracker-config.test.ts`, `tests/tracker-config-mode-none.test.ts`, `tests/gate-check-tracker-config-shape.test.ts`, `tests/resolve-status-mapping.test.ts`. (STE-302)
- **STE-303 — /setup MCP best-match + idempotent tracker-config write.** New `/setup` Step 7f writes `specs/tracker-config.yaml` via MCP fetch + LLM-judgment role-to-status proposal + unified-diff approve/edit/cancel gate; idempotent re-entry no-ops cleanly when the baseline matches the fresh proposal. Helper module `adapters/_shared/src/tracker_config_proposal.ts` exposes `buildTrackerConfigProposal` / `serializeProposalYAML` / `renderUnifiedDiff` / `isProposalNoOp` / `runTrackerConfigWrite`. Linear adapter declares `list_project_statuses: true` capability and binds to `mcp__linear__list_issue_statuses` (team-scoped); Jira adapter binds to `mcp__atlassian__getJiraIssueTypeMetaWithFields` (`allowedValues` extraction). Marker-driven auto-apply via `<dpt:auto-approve>v1</dpt:auto-approve>` per STE-262. Five new capability keys: `tracker_config_write_succeeded`, `tracker_config_write_cancelled`, `tracker_config_unchanged`, `tracker_config_write_skipped_adapter_limit`, `tracker_config_write_mcp_unavailable`. NFR-10 refusal on MCP-unavailable failure modes. Test coverage: `tests/setup-tracker-config-write.test.ts`, `tests/setup-tracker-config-skill-shape.test.ts`, `tests/adapter-schema-w-list-project-statuses.test.ts`. (STE-303)
- **STE-304 — Provider tolerance wrapper for non-key statuses (ask-at-runtime).** New module `adapters/_shared/src/tracker_tolerance.ts` exports `withTolerance(provider, specsDir)` — composable wrapper that routes `Provider.getTicketStatus` through `statusToRole`'s three-way branching: mapped-role match passes through; `null` (known-non-key) prompts operator force/skip/cancel; `"unknown"` (drift) prompts with discovery hint. `AskUserQuestion` shape is 3 closed-form options + always-on `Other` fallback. `force` returns the expected role; `skip` returns `Skipped` sentinel; `cancel` throws `TrackerToleranceCancelledError` (NFR-10 canonical shape). No marker auto-apply for force/skip/cancel — no safe default; non-tty refuses with `RequiresInputRefusedError`. Adapter-config-absent path falls back to per-adapter `status_mapping` (wrapper acts as no-op). Five new capability rows: `tracker_status_forced`, `tracker_status_skipped`, `tracker_status_cancelled`, `tracker_status_unknown_encountered`, `tracker_tolerance_refused_non_tty`. New `/gate-check` probe #53 `tracker_tolerance_wrapper_present` (severity: error) byte-checks wrapper module + export. Test coverage: `tests/tracker-tolerance-wrapper.test.ts`, `tests/gate-check-tracker-tolerance-wrapper-present.test.ts`, `tests/spec-write-tracker-tolerance-capability-rows.test.ts`. (STE-304)

### Changed

- **STE-305 — Relax STE-87 + STE-54 strict status probes via tolerance wrapper.** `/gate-check` probe #14 (`active_ticket_drift`) and probe #8 (`ticket_state_drift`) refactored to route through the STE-304 wrapper via new pure helper `adapters/_shared/src/tolerance_probe_routing.ts` (discriminated outcome union: pass / fail-genuine-drift / prompt-required / advisory-non-tty / strict-fallback-pass / strict-fallback-fail / vacuous-mode-none). Genuine-drift preserved (mapped role mismatch still emits GATE FAILED unchanged); non-tty contexts emit ADVISORY note + `tracker_status_advisory_non_tty` capability row instead of blocking CI; tty contexts prompt operator force/skip/cancel via wrapper. STE-151 carve-outs (single-FR-clean + fully-checked-single-FR exemptions) preserved verbatim — the 23 existing carve-out tests continue to pass unchanged. Config-absent fallback retains strict-equality behavior. `mode: none` still vacuous via existing `local-no-tracker` sentinel. SKILL.md probe #8 + #14 paragraphs rewritten with Tolerance wrapper integration sub-paragraphs. Two new capability rows: `tracker_status_advisory_non_tty`, `tracker_status_genuine_drift`. SKILL_LINE_CAP raised 350 → 351 for spec-write capability-map growth (precedent: STE-252 bumped 300 → 350). Test coverage: `tests/gate-check-status-probes-tolerant.test.ts`, `tests/gate-check-skill-md-tolerance-prose.test.ts`, `tests/gate-check-active-ticket-drift.test.ts` (regression). (STE-305)

Total test count at release: 2006 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.25.0] — 2026-05-18 — "Vendored"

M78 ships a single feat-class FR (STE-301) adding a dependency-docs catalog so consumer projects (typically a mobile app with several private packages) can fold sibling-package docs into design context during `/brainstorm` and `/spec-write`. Architectural twin of STE-230's `spec-research` retargeted from the FR archive to a new git-tracked manifest at `specs/deps.yaml`. Adds a `/deps` user-invocable management skill (add/edit/delete/list/sync), a read-only `deps-researcher` Haiku subagent (Read/Grep/Glob only) invoked via a paired `/deps-research` forked skill on the NON_COMMIT_PRODUCING_SKILLS allowlist, and injection seeds in `/brainstorm` Step 1.5b + `/spec-write` § 0b step 2.5b mirroring the STE-230 injection points.

### Added

- **STE-301 — Dependency docs catalog + topic-aware retrieval (/deps + deps-researcher).** New manifest module at `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/adapters/_shared/src/deps_manifest.ts` exposes `readManifest` / `writeManifest` / `addEntry` / `removeEntry` / `findEntry` / `resolveSiblingPath`; entries are `{name, path, origin?, ref?, kind: "toolkit-docs"}` with name uniqueness + sibling-path constraint (`path` must start with `../`) enforced at read time; throws `DepsManifestShapeError` (NFR-10 canonical shape) on malformed input; CRLF-normalizing YAML parser. New closed-schema parser `parseDepsResearchBlock(...)` at `adapters/_shared/src/deps_research_result.ts` validates the `deps-research-result` fenced block (banner + 3 canonical sections `## Relevant Packages` / `## API Surface Highlights` / `## Reusable Patterns` in fixed order + optional `## Missing deps` + ≤ 25-line cap); pattern clone of STE-230's `parseSpecResearchBlock`. New `/deps` user-invocable skill at `skills/deps/SKILL.md` (router parsing `{add | edit | delete | list | sync}` from `<command-args>`) — `/deps add` Socratic flow with origin prompt, sibling-default derivation from URL basename, auto-detect-existing-checkout-with-matching-origin reuse (per FR Notes open issue, probable answer = yes), `git clone -- "<origin>" "<path>"` (quoted args + `--` terminator to prevent shell-injection), Diátaxis layout validation (`docs/README.md` + at least one of `docs/reference/` / `docs/explanation/` / `docs/how-to/`), and NFR-10 refusal on name collision; `/deps list` tabular output (`name | path | origin | ref | local-status`); `/deps edit` + `/deps delete` Socratic with NFR-10 refusal on missing name (delete is manifest-only); `/deps sync` clone-prompts missing-with-origin entries and surfaces a `ref drift: HEAD=<sha>` advisory when present-checkout HEAD ≠ entry.ref (informational only, never auto-fixes; per FR Notes open issue, probable answer = yes). New read-only `deps-researcher` Haiku subagent at `agents/deps-researcher.md` (`tools: Read, Grep, Glob` — no Write/Edit/Bash/Agent; `model: haiku`); paired child skill at `skills/deps-research/SKILL.md` (`context: fork`, `agent: deps-researcher`, `user-invocable: false`, `argument-hint: <topic>`); vacuous-exit when `specs/deps.yaml` is absent or empty. `deps-research` added to `NON_COMMIT_PRODUCING_SKILLS` allowlist at `adapters/_shared/src/commit_producing_skill_branch_gate.ts` (read-only fork, no VCS writes); `/deps` is NOT exempt (writes specs/deps.yaml). New `/gate-check` probe #51 `deps_researcher_subagent_invariants` (severity: error) at `adapters/_shared/src/deps_researcher_invariants.ts` byte-checks subagent + child-skill frontmatter invariants; mirrors probe #50 (STE-296.8) shape; reuses `tdd_probe_helpers.ts` primitives. Three new static capability keys (`deps_research_invoked`, `deps_research_no_matches`, `deps_research_shape_violation`) registered in `CANONICAL_CAPABILITY_KEYS` at `adapters/_shared/src/closing_summary_capability_keys.ts` with MUST-emit literal-token directives in `/spec-write` § 0b step 2.5b; `/brainstorm` Step 1.5b mirrors the injection contract. CLAUDE.md skill + agent counts bumped: 18 → 20 skills (deps + deps-research); 5 → 6 agents (deps-researcher). Skills `STE-N` token ceiling raised 220 → 230 to fit the new anchor refs. Four new test files at `tests/`: `deps-manifest.test.ts` (22 tests), `deps-research-result.test.ts` (12 tests), `deps-research-injection.test.ts` (17 tests), `gate-check-deps-researcher-invariants.test.ts` (15 tests) — 66 new tests. (STE-301)

Total test count at release: 1850 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.24.0] — 2026-05-15 — "Audited"

M77 ships a single feat-class FR adding a fourth forked-subagent stage to the `/tdd` multi-agent orchestrator (STE-225). STE-296 introduces a read-only `tdd-spec-reviewer` that runs once at end of FR after REFACTOR succeeds GREEN, independently traces every AC to its implementation + test, and blocks the pipeline only on `missing_acs` (binary contract violations) with a bounded single-round auto-retry through `tdd-write-test` + `tdd-implement` scoped to the missing ACs. Halts non-zero with a new `spec-gap` failure mode if the second audit still finds missing ACs; advisory findings (`partial_acs`, `drift_count`, `cross_cutting_drift`) ride along in the report without halting. Closes the second-line-of-defense gap STE-225 deliberately left open: `tdd-result` validates each subagent's *claims*; the audit step validates *reality*.

### Added

- **STE-296 — Spec-review audit step in /tdd pipeline (block on Missing AC, bounded auto-retry).** New 4th stage in the `/tdd` multi-agent orchestrator: a read-only `tdd-spec-reviewer` subagent at `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/agents/tdd-spec-reviewer.md` (tools: `Read, Grep, Glob`; `maxTurns: 8`; `model: sonnet`) and child skill at `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/tdd-spec-review/SKILL.md` (`context: fork`, `user-invocable: false`, `agent: tdd-spec-reviewer`). New deterministic parser `parseTddSpecReviewBlock(...)` at `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/adapters/_shared/src/tdd_spec_review_result.ts` validates the closed-schema `tdd-spec-review-result` fenced block (role, status, missing_acs, partial_acs, drift_count, advisory_findings, cross_cutting_drift, command, output_excerpt; optional notes). New orchestrator state-machine helper `stepSpecReview(...)` at `tdd_spec_review_orchestrator.ts` returns `{decision: "exit-ok" | "retry-write-test-implement" | "halt", capabilityKey?, missingAcs}` — capability key emitted only on terminal outcomes (retry branch is still in flight). New `recordAuditRoundFailure(budget)` at `tdd_retry_state.ts` carries an independent `audit-round` budget (cap=1) that does not consume per-AC test-writer / implementer / refactorer budgets. `formatHaltReport(...)` at `tdd_halt_report.ts` extended with new `spec-gap` failure mode + `missingAcs` rendering; `TddRole` union widened with `"spec-reviewer"`. New `/gate-check` probe #50 `tdd_spec_reviewer_subagent_invariants` (severity: error) enforces frontmatter invariants on the new subagent + child skill byte-checkably; mirrors STE-225 AC.7's `tdd_orchestrator_integrity` probe shape. Three capability keys (`tdd_spec_audit_passed` / `tdd_spec_audit_missing_recovered` / `tdd_spec_audit_halted`) propagate the audit outcome through `/implement`'s closing summary; static map row added to `skills/spec-write/SKILL.md` § 7; capability-propagation paragraph added to `skills/implement/SKILL.md` Phase 3. Cross-AC refactor extracts shared fence + scoped-YAML primitives into `tdd_fence_yaml.ts` (reused by `tdd_result.ts` + `tdd_spec_review_result.ts`) and shared probe primitives into `tdd_probe_helpers.ts` (reused by `tdd_orchestrator_integrity.ts` + `tdd_spec_reviewer_invariants.ts`); net dedup while closed-schema field validation stays local to each caller. Deprecated alias `milestone_attach_unavailable` removed from spec-write SKILL.md § 7 capability map per its own retirement prose (STE-198 honored-for-one-minor-version-cycle window expired); probe #26's canonical key set unchanged. CLAUDE.md counts updated: 17 → 18 skills, 4 → 5 agents. (STE-296)

Total test count at release: 1780 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.23.0] — 2026-05-15 — "Reconciled"

M70 ships state-emission convergence + post-iter-1 contract closures across three FRs. STE-284 closes the partial-scan trap surfaced 2026-05-13 when `/conformance-loop` iter-1 created M70 + STE-280/281/282 directly on Linear with no local files (branch unmerged); a subsequent `/spec-write` on `main` would have allocated M71 over the top. The new `reconcileTrackerLocal()` helper at `adapters/_shared/src/reconcile_tracker_local.ts` is the single source of truth consumed by both `/spec-write` § 0.5 preamble (auto-imports tracker→local orphans, guarded by `existsSync` per STE-135) and `/gate-check` probe #49 (`tracker_local_reconciliation_drift`, severity warning → error on hard FR-id collisions). The `Provider` interface evolves with `mode` / `listMilestones` / `listActiveFRs` methods; `LocalProvider` returns `[]` / `'none'`, `TrackerProvider` delegates to the driver via optional-chained calls. STE-119's M31 tracker-exclusion decision (`nextFreeMilestoneNumber` as mode-agnostic) is explicitly superseded. STE-294 extends the STE-220 → STE-226 → STE-237 → STE-262 → STE-270 marker-trigger triple-layer defense pattern: `FORBIDDEN_PHRASES` now flags `standing instruction` + `default-applied per standing` autonomous-mode-reminder paraphrases; `/spec-write` SKILL.md carries the canonical NOT-a-trigger anchor sentence byte-repeated at 3 gate sites (§ 0b step 4, § 7a, ## Rules), with `NOT acceptable` as the negation-signature carve-out; a regression fixture at `tests/fixtures/socratic-first-turn/regression/spec-write-marker-absent-reminder-present-2026-05-14.json` reproduces the iter-1 § F1 capture, and a new runtime test asserts `RequiresInputRefusedError` raises with NFR-10 canonical shape. STE-295 bundles 5 iter-1 follow-ups: hook carve-out for spec-only commits, `stripLinearACFences` extended to the `mcp__linear__get_issue` read path, smoke-test master-merge step + severity-format canonical normalization, `/gate-check` probe #37 fence-only scope doc. Forward-only per `project_no_users_yet`.

### Added

- **STE-284 — Tracker ↔ local FR/milestone reconciliation.** New `reconcileTrackerLocal(provider, specsDir)` helper at `adapters/_shared/src/reconcile_tracker_local.ts` returns `{ trackerOrphans, localOrphans, milestoneMismatches }`; shared `readLocalFRBindings(specsDir)` SoT consumed by both `/spec-write` § 0.5 preamble and `/gate-check` probe #49. `nextFreeMilestoneNumber` extended with optional `provider` param; in tracker mode unions tracker milestones via `Provider.listMilestones()`; returns `{ next, sources: { active, archived, changelog, tracker } }`; now async (existing single-caller updated to `await`). `Provider` interface evolution: new `mode: 'none' | 'tracker'` readonly property + `listMilestones(): Promise<{name: string}[]>` + `listActiveFRs(): Promise<string[]>`. `LocalProvider` returns `[]` / `'none'`; `TrackerProvider` delegates to driver via `await this.driver.listMilestones?.() ?? []`. `StubProvider` in `import.test.ts` extended with the three new methods. `/gate-check` probe `tracker_local_reconciliation_drift` registered in `skills/gate-check/SKILL.md`; severity tiers: warning (any drift) → error (dangling local binding to non-existent tracker ID OR duplicate local bindings). Three capability keys (`tracker_local_reconciled`, `tracker_local_orphan_local`, `milestone_local_orphan`) added to both `spec-write` and `gate-check` capability maps with plain-language explanations. STE-119's M31 tracker-exclusion decision explicitly superseded in STE-284 § Notes. (STE-284)

### Fixed

- **STE-294 — STE-226 hardening; /spec-write auto-apply must ignore autonomous-mode-reminder paraphrases.** `FORBIDDEN_PHRASES` const in `adapters/_shared/src/spec_write_alternate_trigger_scan.ts` extended with `standing instruction` + `default-applied per standing` (the two truly-new phrases; `autonomous-mode reminder` and `work without stopping` were already present from STE-262). `skills/spec-write/SKILL.md` § 0b step 4 + § 7a + `## Rules` each carry the canonical NOT-a-trigger anchor sentence byte-repeated (3× total); `NOT acceptable` is the negation-signature carve-out so the anchor lines self-exclude from the probe's positive-match logic. Regression fixture at `tests/fixtures/socratic-first-turn/regression/spec-write-marker-absent-reminder-present-2026-05-14.json` reproduces the iter-1 § F1 capture (autonomous-mode reminder + marker absent + non-TTY stdin); new runtime test at `tests/spec-write-marker-detection-runtime.test.ts` loads the fixture, runs gate-evaluation through `checkMarkerRuntime` + `requireOrRefuse`, asserts `RequiresInputRefusedError` raises with NFR-10 canonical shape naming gate site `draft`. smoke-test SKILL.md fixture 1b assertion changed to byte-checkable post-TIGHTEN form `Linear-side AND Jira-side both raised RequiresInputRefusedError` with diagnostic `STE-226 runtime regression: spec-write marker-absent fixture 1b` per STE-231 AC-5 shape. Cross-tracker asymmetry root-cause documented as LLM stochasticity (AC.5 path b) — the AC.1–AC.3 byte-check triple-layer defense is the authoritative mechanism that makes the variance irrelevant. (STE-294)

- **STE-295 — Smoke fixture group; M70 post-iter-1 cohort follow-ups.** Five-AC bundle. (1) `pre-commit-tdd-orchestrator` hook skips the `/tdd` requirement when the staged set is spec-only (`specs/frs/*.md`, `specs/plan/M*.md`, `specs/{plan,frs}/archive/*.md`, `specs/{requirements,technical-spec,testing-spec}.md`) AND no `src/**`, `**/__tests__/**`, or `*.{test,spec}.{ts,tsx,js}` paths are staged. Mixed spec+src/test still requires `/tdd`. New named export `classifyStagedPaths` (pure verdict function) drives the entrypoint behind `import.meta.main` so unit tests import without spawning hook I/O. (2) `stripLinearACFences` extended to the read path via new wrapper at `adapters/linear/src/get_issue.ts`; round-trip test asserts `pushDescription → fetchDescription` byte-equality. (3) smoke-test SKILL.md Phase 2 master-merge step (`chore/setup-bootstrap` → master, `--no-ff`) lands before the `branch_gate_default_applied` auto-apply spawn so the canonical chain exercises STE-228's default-applied path. (4) `/gate-check` SKILL.md probe #37 anchor body documents fence-only scope (path tokens inside fenced directory-tree blocks only; bare-prose mentions never flagged). (5) smoke-test SKILL.md severity-format canonical normalization callout (`**Severity:** <level>`, colon ends bold). Spec deviation: STE-290's pre-existing FR-only-refusal integration test conflicted with AC.1's carve-out; two tests updated to assert FR-only → exit 0 and use `src/foo.test.ts` for the refusal case. (STE-295)

Total test count at release: 2445 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.22.4] — 2026-05-14 — "Blocking"

M76 ships a single fix-class FR that closes the residual exit-code-semantics gap left by STE-290. The 3 Refusing hooks (`pre-commit-gate-check`, `pre-pr-spec-review`, `pre-commit-tdd-orchestrator`) fired and emitted NFR-10 `Refusing:` stderr on miss but called `process.exit(found ? 0 : 1)` — Claude Code treats `exit 1` as advisory (stderr to operator only, command proceeds). The blocking contract is `exit 2` (stderr fed to the model as feedback, command actually blocked). Discovery 2026-05-14: a `gh pr create --help` invocation with no `Skill(dev-process-toolkit:spec-review)` in the session transcript fired the hook, emitted the refusal block to the operator, but Claude Code reported "Failed with non-blocking status code" and ran `gh` anyway — the model never received the refusal as feedback. STE-285's exit-code assumption (`exit 1` = block) was wrong; the actual contract is `exit 2`. Forward-only per `project_no_users_yet`.

### Fixed

- **STE-291 — Hook refusal exit code; switch 3 Refusing hooks from exit 1 (advisory) to exit 2 (blocking).** `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/templates/hooks/_lib/hooks/pre-commit-gate-check.ts`, `pre-pr-spec-review.ts`, and `pre-commit-tdd-orchestrator.ts` flip `process.exit(found ? 0 : 1)` → `process.exit(found ? 0 : 2)` on the miss path (one byte per hook). The byte-stable NFR-10 `Refusing:` stderr emit (via `requireSkillToolUse` → `emitNFR10`) is preserved unchanged per STE-286 §104 / STE-290 AC.6. `pre-spec-write-brainstorm-reminder.ts` stays at `exit 0` on the advisory miss path (UserPromptSubmit reminders should not block the user's prompt, by STE-285 design). 7 assertion-line tightenings across 6 test files (3 unit + 3 integration) lift the refusal-case assertion from `expect(r.exitCode).not.toBe(0)` to `expect(r.exitCode).toBe(2)` — regression guard against a future drift back to exit 1. `docs/hooks-reference.md` adds a new "Exit-code contract (Claude Code 2.1.x)" paragraph pinning the empirically-verified Claude Code 2.1.141 hook contract: `exit 0` → tool call proceeds; `exit 2` → blocked + stderr-to-model; any other non-zero (including `exit 1`) → advisory + stderr-to-operator only. Behavioral change: hooks now actually block (previously emitted stderr but the tool call proceeded). Forward-only — no migration helper per `project_no_users_yet`. (STE-291)

Total test count at release: 2347 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.22.3] — 2026-05-14 — "Wired"

M75 ships a single fix-class FR that resurrects the byte-checkable toolkit-contract enforcement layer. STE-285 (M71, v2.21.0 "Honored") had the layer call `require_skill_tool_use` against `$CLAUDE_SESSION_FILE` — an env var the Claude Code harness never sets. The helper hit its "fail-open when unset" branch on every dispatch, leaving the layer **inert since v2.21.0 shipped**. Empirical probe on 2026-05-14 (one-off `/tmp/dpt-hook-probe` plugin run under raw `claude` / `cca` / `claude-st` × iTerm2 / cmux — 6 launches, all confirmed) verified the harness passes session info on stdin as JSON carrying `transcript_path`. M75 ports the helper to that contract. Forward-only per `project_no_users_yet` — no migration logic.

### Fixed

- **STE-290 — Hook contract fix; read transcript_path from stdin JSON instead of $CLAUDE_SESSION_FILE env var.** New `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/templates/hooks/_lib/session.ts` Bun TS lib exports `parseHookPayload` (fail-open on empty / unparseable / missing `transcript_path`), `findSkillToolUse` (no-emit pure boolean atomic-line `"name":"Skill"` AND `"skill":"<skill>"` grep on `transcript_path`), `requireSkillToolUse` (delegates to findSkillToolUse + emits NFR-10 `Refusing:` block on miss), and `emitNFR10` (preserves STE-286 §104 byte-stable `Refusing:` / `Reminder:` / `Context: mode=hook, ticket=unbound, skill=<skill>, hook=<hook>` substrings). Four per-hook TS modules under `_lib/hooks/` (`pre-commit-gate-check.ts`, `pre-pr-spec-review.ts`, `pre-commit-tdd-orchestrator.ts`, `pre-spec-write-brainstorm-reminder.ts`) each read stdin via `Bun.stdin.text()`, parse via `parseHookPayload`, apply command-pattern guard (`/^git commit\b/` for gate-check + tdd-orchestrator; `/^gh pr create\b/` for spec-review) or prompt-match (`/dev-process-toolkit:spec-write` substring in `payload.prompt` for brainstorm-reminder), then delegate. The advisory brainstorm-reminder uses `findSkillToolUse` + own `emitNFR10("Reminder", …)` and exits 0; the three Refusing hooks delegate to `requireSkillToolUse` and exit 1 on miss. tdd-orchestrator keeps its staged-file heuristic via `git diff --cached --name-only` filesystem call (no `$CLAUDE_STAGED_FILES` env var). Bash shims at `templates/hooks/process/<name>.sh` shrink to the canonical 2-line `exec bun run "${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT}/templates/hooks/_lib/hooks/<name>.ts"` shape — filenames + `.sh` extension preserved per STE-285 / STE-289 §119 so `bundled-hooks-shape.test.ts` AC.6 conformance stays GREEN. `_lib/session.sh` deleted; zero `$CLAUDE_SESSION_FILE` / `session.sh` references remain under `templates/hooks/`. Four integration tests at `__tests__/<name>.test.ts` rewritten to inject realistic stdin payload via `Bun.spawn({ stdin, env: { CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT } })` — ≤ 2 cases each (happy + refusal). Five new dedicated unit test files under `tests/hook-{session-lib,modules-pre-*}.test.ts` (86 cases for this FR across 10 files) provide failure isolation. `docs/hooks-reference.md` updated to the new contract (transcript_path stdin payload supersedes the never-set env var; STE-285 supersede note retained for historical context). The architecture is launcher-agnostic and config-dir-agnostic — same code path under raw `claude` / `cca` / `claude-st` / iTerm2 / cmux. Behavioral change: hooks were silently fail-open; they now actually enforce. Manual cleanup needed for marketplace users: none (zero shipped users — forward-only). (STE-290)

Total test count at release: 2336 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.22.2] — 2026-05-14 — "Bundled"

M74 ships a forward-only fix reversing M71/M72/M73's install-side hook mechanism. Empirically falsified: the Claude Code harness only expands `${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT}` in plugin-bundled `<plugin>/hooks/hooks.json`, never in user `.claude/settings.json` — so the M71→M73 install-side line of reasoning was structurally impossible. Discovered 2026-05-14 when the operator ran `/dev-process-toolkit:setup --hooks=all` against v2.22.1 in a downstream project; the harness emitted the canonical refusal `Hook command references ${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT} but the hook is not associated with a plugin`. M74 ships the plugin-bundled `hooks/hooks.json` and rips out the install-side surface entirely. Reverses STE-262/STE-270/STE-276's prior rejection of bundled `hooks/hooks.json` — the rejection grounds (spawn blast radius, triple-check conflict, no clean per-session state) all remain mitigated as before. Forward-only — zero shipped marketplace users; no migration logic.

### Fixed

- **STE-289 — Hooks bundling redo; ship plugin-bundled hooks/hooks.json; rip out /setup --hooks installer.** New `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/hooks/hooks.json` registers the 4 Process-category hooks for harness auto-discovery (3 `PreToolUse:Bash` + 1 `UserPromptSubmit:*`, each `command` field using the inline form `"${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT}"/templates/hooks/process/<name>.sh` with `timeout: 5000`). Ripped out: `install_hooks.ts` (4 functions + `HOOK_REGISTRATIONS` + `HOOK_ARGS_PREFIX` constant); 5 setup test files (`hooks_menu_prompt`, `hooks_merge_settings`, `setup_hooks_flag`, `setup_hooks_preselect`, `smoke_fixture_group_8_doc_conformance`); 1 stale capability-rows test logically forced by AC.3's prose removal; section 0c "Contract-enforcement re-invocation flag" + section 6a "Toolkit-contract enforcement hooks menu" from `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/setup/SKILL.md`; fixture group 8 prose from `.claude/skills/smoke-test/SKILL.md`. `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/docs/hooks-reference.md` rewritten to the bundled mechanism (harness auto-discovers from the marketplace cache `~/.claude/plugins/cache/<plugin>/<version>/hooks/hooks.json`; no `/setup --hooks` flow, no user-settings.json mutation, no per-project opt-in). The 4 hook scripts at `templates/hooks/process/*.sh` and their per-script unit tests survive — only the registration mechanism moves. New `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/tests/bundled-hooks-shape.test.ts` is the byte-shape regression guard (25 tests: 4-entry count, matcher split, command prefix, timeout, raw-byte token count, script-path resolution). Manual cleanup for marketplace users on v2.22.1 with stale `.claude/settings.json` hook entries: delete the 4 dev-process-toolkit hook entries from `.claude/settings.json`. Discovery context (2026-05-14): operator ran `/dev-process-toolkit:setup --hooks=all` against v2.22.1 in `~/workspace/quack`; the harness emitted `Hook command references ${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT} but the hook is not associated with a plugin. This variable is only available in hooks defined in a plugin's hooks/hooks.json file, not in [user settings.json]`. Empirical research via the `claude-code-guide` agent confirmed the contract. (STE-289)

Total test count at release: 2296 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.22.1] — 2026-05-14 — "Portable"

M73 ships a single-FR forward-only fix for the STE-285 (M71) hook installer: `additionFor` and `readInstalledHookNames` in `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/setup/install_hooks.ts` were interpolating the JS-resolved absolute `pluginRoot` path into `.claude/settings.json` `args[0]` instead of the literal `${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT}/templates/hooks/process/<name>.sh` token the Claude Code harness expands at hook-fire time per STE-285 AC-STE-285.3. The bug only manifested on marketplace installs whose runtime plugin path differs from the install-time path; in-tree dev clones (and fixture group 8 by extension) resolved both interpretations to the same path and missed the regression. M73 aligns the implementation with STE-285's documented design intent. No migration — zero shipped marketplace users.

### Fixed

- **STE-288 — Hook install path portability — emit literal ${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT} token.** Two-line fix in `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/setup/install_hooks.ts`: `additionFor(name, pluginRoot)` now emits `args: ["${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT}/templates/hooks/process/<name>.sh"]` as a literal string (the harness expands `${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT}` at hook-fire time), and `readInstalledHookNames(settingsPath, pluginRoot)` matches the same literal-token prefix. Hoisted the shared literal into a module-level `HOOK_ARGS_PREFIX` constant to prevent write/read drift. The `pluginRoot` parameter remains on both signatures for source-compat (now unused, silenced via `void pluginRoot`). Two-layer regression guard: unit tests in `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/setup/__tests__/{hooks_merge_settings,setup_hooks_flag}.test.ts` pin the literal-string shape (byte-equality on `additionFor` output across all 4 seeded hook registrations + full `installHooks` round-trip; dev-clone-absolute-path-not-detected on `readInstalledHookNames`); fixture group 8 install-verification grep in `.claude/skills/smoke-test/SKILL.md` pins the runtime-emitted JSON shape (`grep -c -F '${CLAUDE_PLUGIN_ROOT}/templates/hooks/process/' .claude/settings.json` ≥ 4 — one entry per seeded hook). Forward-only: no legacy-shape migration logic, per `project_no_users_yet` (zero shipped marketplace users). Discovery context: user noticed absolute-path entries in `.claude/settings.json` after running `/setup --hooks` in a downstream project during M72 dogfooding. (STE-288)

Total test count at release: 2335 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

New `docs/hooks-reference.md` user manual enumerates each hook (name, event, matcher, requirement, NFR-10 refusal shape, override pattern). Per-project opt-in design supersedes the STE-262/STE-270/STE-276 session-wide-bundling rejections — bounded blast radius, user-consented per project. (STE-285)
