## [2.20.0] — 2026-05-11 — "Byte-Strict"

M69 ships the third attempt at the `/spec-write` marker gate (STE-213/M55 prose-only, STE-220/M56 prose-only, STE-226/M59 marker-mechanism). Each prior attempt was falsified by subsequent smoke runs: the LLM imputed the marker from the harness's autonomous-mode reminder ("work without stopping") or from `claude -p` non-interactive inference, conflating prose context with the byte-checkable token. STE-262 introduces a runtime byte-grep helper that turns the gate decision into a deterministic Bash precheck — the SKILL.md gate sites invoke a CLI shim, branch strictly on its stdout (`PRESENT` / `ABSENT`), and never infer at the LLM layer. STE-270 hardens the parallel STE-251 first-turn contract for `/spec-write` (where `/conformance-loop` iter-1 on 2026-05-10 caught a new violation despite the prose mandate). Both FRs apply the recurring lesson: byte-checkable / structural enforcement at the source-level + runtime layer, not prose-only mandates.

### Added

- **STE-262 — Tighten /spec-write commit-gate + draft-gate to literal byte-checkable marker only.** New pure-fn helper `adapters/_shared/src/check_marker_runtime.ts` exports `checkMarkerRuntime(promptBody): { present: boolean }` — case-sensitive 39-byte literal substring match, no regex, no whitespace tolerance, no version flexibility. CLI shim accepts `<file-path>` or `-` (stdin) and prints `PRESENT` / `ABSENT` on a single stdout line; exits non-zero on I/O errors with NFR-10 canonical error message. `/spec-write` SKILL.md gate sites (§ 0b step 4 + § 7a) invoke the helper via Bash BEFORE evaluating the auto-apply branch and branch strictly on its stdout — marker `ABSENT` + non-tty → `RequiresInputRefusedError`; marker-PRESENT path byte-identical. New `/gate-check` probe #48 `spec_write_marker_alternate_trigger_scan` (severity: error) at `adapters/_shared/src/spec_write_alternate_trigger_scan.ts` globs ONLY `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/spec-write/SKILL.md` and scans for 6 literal forbidden alternate-trigger paraphrases (`Auto Mode`, `work without stopping`, `imputed approval`, `autonomous-mode reminder`, `inferred approval`, `non-interactive inference`) with byte-checkable negation-context carve-outs (`single deterministic`, `are removed`/`is removed`, `regardless of`, `NOT acceptable`) for legitimate negation/historical references. New `tests/spec-write-marker-strict-runtime.test.ts` simulates the gate-site flow in-process (no real `claude -p` spawn). Backward compatibility: marker PRESENT (any stdin) byte-identical; marker ABSENT + tty unchanged; marker ABSENT + non-tty changes from silent commit (the BUG) to loud refusal. Triple-check posture (per user directive 2026-05-08 "we shouldn't ruin plugin functionality! Every change in the plugin itself should be triple-checked before implementing!") operationalized via per-AC unit + integration smoke + manual diff review at the three load-bearing files. (STE-262)
- **STE-270 — Lock /spec-write Pattern 26 first-turn contract: regression fixture + drift probe + protocol clarification.** Hardening of STE-251 (M67), parallel to how STE-262 hardens STE-226. New regression baseline fixture pinned at `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/tests/fixtures/socratic-first-turn/regression/spec-write-2026-05-10.json` capturing the `/conformance-loop` iter-1 (2026-05-10) Phase 8 violation transcript (`Write@19` before any `AskUserQuestion`). New replay test `socratic_first_turn_replay_2026_05_10.test.ts` re-feeds the fixture through `parseStreamJsonTranscript` + `assertFirstTurnShape` and asserts violation captured with `toolName === "Write"`, `index === 19`, message references `docs/auto-mode-protocol.md`. New `/gate-check` probe #47 `spec_write_first_turn_drift_scan` (severity: error) at `adapters/_shared/src/spec_write_first_turn_drift_scan.ts` mirrors STE-262's `spec_write_alternate_trigger_scan.ts` — globs ONLY `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/spec-write/SKILL.md` and scans for 6 literal forbidden first-turn-drift paraphrases (`pre-baked args allow`, `verbose <command-args> permits`, `autonomous-mode permits skip`, `marker absence implies`, `first AskUserQuestion may be deferred`, `Socratic loop is optional under`). `/spec-write` SKILL.md line 12 strengthened with the literal hardening sentence (pre-baked args, autonomous-mode reminder, and marker absence are NOT acceptable triggers to skip the first `AskUserQuestion`). `docs/auto-mode-protocol.md § Socratic Loop Contract` updated with the matching one-line clarification. Cross-skill non-regression guard: the existing STE-251 `socratic_first_turn_replay.test.ts` (2026-05-07 fixture) continues to PASS unchanged. Two regression baselines (2026-05-07 + 2026-05-10) now preserve forward-compat across future SKILL.md edits. (STE-270)

Total test count at release: 2235 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.19.0] — 2026-05-08 — "Allowlist"

M68 replaces the blanket `--permission-mode bypassPermissions` posture across the `/conformance-loop` call tree with a tracked, content-rich `permissions.allow` allow-list in `.claude/settings.json`. The toolkit's "policy artifact" goes from constraint-by-presence (the file exists, so the bypass is acceptable) to constraint-by-content (the file enumerates exactly what the call tree may invoke, reviewable in PR diffs). Children spawn in default permission mode and honor the allow-list at command-pattern granularity (Bash patterns, Edit/Write/Read/Grep/Glob, MCP tool families). The release also lands six baseline cleanups (`requirements.md` version line bump, marker-probe carve-out for Phase 8 socratic-loop fixtures, tracked `.mcp.json` + `package.json` with `ts-morph` devDep, gate-check / setup SKILL.md cap trims, NFR-1 cap bumped from 300 → 350 lines) so `/ship-milestone`'s baseline-test gate is clean for the first time since v2.16.0.

### Added

- **STE-252 — Replace bypassPermissions with tracked permissions.allow in /conformance-loop call-tree.** Tracked `.claude/settings.json` carries a 22-entry `permissions.allow` block (Bash command patterns: `bun:*`, `bun test:*`, `git:*`, `gh:*`, `find:*`, `realpath:*`, `mkdir:*`, `rm:*`, `cat:*`, `wc:*`, `wait`, `kill`, `cp:*`, `ls:*`, `tee:*`; file tools: `Edit`, `Write`, `Read`, `Grep`, `Glob`; MCP families: `mcp__linear__*`, `mcp__atlassian__*`), lex-sorted for byte-stable diffs. `--permission-mode bypassPermissions` removed from every `claude -p` spawn fence in `.claude/skills/conformance-loop/SKILL.md` (4 sites: Phase A `/smoke-test` pair + Phase B `/spec-write` + `/implement`) and `.claude/skills/smoke-test/SKILL.md` (5 fences across Phase 2 non-prompt children, prompt-bearing setup/spec-write/implement, and the Phase 8 stream-json wrapper); default-mode spawns rely on the tracked allow-list. New `/conformance-loop` Phase 0 pre-flight (f) JSON-parses `.claude/settings.json`, asserts `.permissions.allow` is a non-empty array, refuses with NFR-10 canonical shape on miss (file + remedy + context), logs `permissions_allow_present` on hit. New `/gate-check` probe #46 `conformance-loop-bypass-removed` (severity: error) globs `.claude/skills/{conformance-loop,smoke-test}/SKILL.md`, finds every fenced `bash` block containing `claude -p `, asserts none carry `--permission-mode bypassPermissions`. Vacuous on toolkit consumers without the project-local skills. Threat-model prose rewritten in both files: `/smoke-test` § Threat model + Path-safety pre-flight #6 demoted from "justifies bypassPermissions" framing to cwd guard; `/conformance-loop` § Path-safety guard delegated to children paragraph names tracked `permissions.allow` as the per-tool-call enforcement mechanism. Refactor: `extractBashFences()` + `BashFence` hoisted from `auto_approve_marker.ts` into shared `markdown_fences.ts`; probes #38 + #46 consume it. Empirical validation (AC-STE-252.5) deferred-acceptance per `feedback_smoke_post_ship_retroactive` — the manual `/conformance-loop --max-iterations 1 --linear-team STE` run lands as a follow-up smoke. (STE-252)

## [2.18.0] — 2026-05-08 — "Hush"

M67 ships round 3 of the autonomous-mode contract hardening sequence (M58 STE-226 marker, M65 STE-232 per-step refusal, M66 STE-237 Socratic-loop entry / STE-238 capability-key emission). STE-251 closes the two surfaces `/conformance-loop` iter-1 (2026-05-08, post-M66-merge) caught: F1 (Pattern 26 entry-side cross-tracker drift — `/spec-write` violates on Linear, `/setup` violates on Jira) + F2 (marker-absent silent-commit path under `claude -p` non-tty stdin — model rationalizes past dismissed `AskUserQuestion` responses and lands real commits via "safe defaults"). Detection-only scope; non-interactive only — interactive (tty) sessions are byte-identical to v2.17.0. M68 candidate: runtime PreToolUse harness hook for F1 enforcement IF M67 detection-only proves insufficient at the next `/conformance-loop` iteration.

### Added

- **STE-251 — Strengthen Pattern-26 first-turn + refusal contracts under non-interactive stdin.** Source-level lead-clause prepend on all four in-scope skill bodies (`plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/{setup,brainstorm,spec-write,report-issue}/SKILL.md`) — "FIRST ACTION (under non-interactive stdin)" forbids `Write` / `Edit` / `NotebookEdit` tool calls before the first `AskUserQuestion` `tool_use` OR `RequiresInputRefusedError` raise; read-only orientation (`Read` / `Grep` / `Glob` / `Bash`-read-only) explicitly allowed; clause cites `docs/auto-mode-protocol.md § Socratic Loop Contract` and carries explicit "non-tty stdin only" qualifier so interactive (tty) invocations stay byte-identical. `requireOrRefuse(...)` at `adapters/_shared/src/require_or_refuse.ts` gains a non-tty branch: when `process.stdin.isTTY === false` AND the gate's required value is missing (the dismissed-AskUserQuestion path that previously fell through to "safe defaults"), throws `RequiresInputRefusedError` with NFR-10 canonical message (gate site + missing value + remedy `re-invoke with --tracker=<mode> pre-bake or run interactively (tty)`); when `isTTY === true`, current behavior preserved unchanged. New `/gate-check` probe `socratic_first_turn_post_hoc_drift` at `adapters/_shared/src/socratic_first_turn_post_hoc_drift.ts` scans the latest commit on the active branch — if commit subject matches the canonical `/spec-write` pattern AND the body contains NEITHER an audit-row marker (`spec_write_draft_default_applied` / `spec_write_commit_default_applied`) NOR a refusal NFR-10 block, surfaces `socratic_first_turn_post_hoc_drift_violation` and hard-fails the gate. The committed F1 reproducer at `tests/fixtures/socratic-first-turn/spec-write-2026-05-07.json` is moved under `tests/fixtures/socratic-first-turn/regression/` to survive per-date overwrites by future Phase 8 runs; new unit test `socratic_first_turn_replay.test.ts` re-feeds it through `parseStreamJsonTranscript` + `assertFirstTurnShape` and asserts the helper still detects it as a violation (forward-compat for the helper's contract). Test coverage: 4-case matrix on `require_or_refuse.test.ts` (tty/answered, tty/declined, non-tty/answered, non-tty/dismissed); fixture matrix on `socratic_first_turn_post_hoc_drift.test.ts` covering canonical-subject + audit-row, canonical-subject + refusal-block, canonical-subject + neither (violation), non-canonical-subject (vacuous); replay test exercising the F1 reproducer. (STE-251)

Total test count at release: 652 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.17.0] — 2026-05-07 — "Socratic"

M66 ships round 2 of the autonomous-mode contract hardening. STE-237 closes the symmetric loop-entry side of STE-232's per-step refusal: under the autonomous-mode reminder + verbose pre-baked-args + no auto-approve marker, the model can skip an entire Socratic clarification loop before any gated step fires (the magpie incident, gist `https://gist.github.com/nesquikm/2904e50c7213b6aa392b998d4137f609`, 2026-05-07, plugin v2.16.0). Universal `AskUserQuestion` mandate (B-side) makes loop-skip structurally impossible; `/smoke-test` Phase 8 + new `/gate-check` probe (C-side) enforces source and behavior. STE-238 closes the byte-checkable-token emission gap caught by `/conformance-loop` iteration 1 (2026-05-07, F1+F3+F4): SKILL.md prose for STE-226 / STE-228 / STE-230 specifies literal capability-key tokens (`spec_write_draft_default_applied`, `branch_gate_default_applied`, `spec_research_invoked`, etc.) but the runtime LLM emits narrative prose, not the tokens. Both FRs share STE-220's lesson — prose-only enforcement drifts; byte-checkable structural verification is required — applied to two surfaces.

### Added

- **STE-237 — Socratic Loop Contract: universal `AskUserQuestion` mandate + first-turn contract.** New `## Socratic Loop Contract` section in `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/docs/auto-mode-protocol.md` immediately after `## Refusal Mechanism` covering (a) the rule (every clarifying Q in a Pattern-26-tagged skill body MUST be emitted as an `AskUserQuestion` tool call regardless of autonomous-mode reminder / auto-approve marker / pre-baked args), (b) the first-turn contract (`Write` / `Edit` / `NotebookEdit` forbidden before the first `AskUserQuestion` `tool_use` OR `RequiresInputRefusedError` raise; `Read` / `Grep` / `Glob` / `Bash`-read-only orientation allowed), (c) the in-scope skill list (initial: `/setup`, `/brainstorm`, `/spec-write`, `/report-issue`; forward-extension hook for `Pattern 26` prose OR `socratic: true` frontmatter), (d) cross-references to STE-226 / STE-232 / STE-220. New pure-I/O helper `assertFirstTurnShape(transcript)` at `adapters/_shared/src/socratic_first_turn.ts` is the single arbiter of the first-turn contract — returns `{ outcome: 'ok-asked' | 'ok-refused' | 'violation', firstScaffoldEntry?, askIndex? }`; throws `SocraticFirstTurnViolationError` (NFR-10 canonical Verdict / Remedy / Context lines) on violation, naming offending tool name + zero-based index. New `/gate-check` probe #43 `socratic_loop_uses_ask_user_question` (severity: error) globs `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/*/SKILL.md` + `.claude/skills/*/SKILL.md`; for every skill body that cites `Pattern 26` OR carries `socratic: true` frontmatter, asserts (i) the body references `AskUserQuestion` AND (ii) cites `docs/auto-mode-protocol.md`; HTML-comment-scoped Pattern-26 mentions are stripped before scanning. New `/smoke-test` Phase 8 — Socratic Loop Entry — spawns `claude -p` children for each in-scope skill carrying the autonomous-mode reminder verbatim + verbose pre-baked-args + NO auto-approve marker; captures the response stream and asserts via `assertFirstTurnShape(...)`; fixture artifacts under `tests/fixtures/socratic-first-turn/`. `## /setup audit` row format gains `loop_entered: true|false` column via `appendAuditRow(...)`'s new `loopEntered: boolean` parameter; pairs with STE-232's `imputed:` for two-axis loop visibility (`imputed:true` flags model-imputed values for gates that DID fire; `loop_entered:false` flags loops that NEVER fired — the magpie regression class). Parser tolerates legacy rows (no `loop_entered:` column ⇒ `loopEntered: undefined`); permutation tests cover every column-presence combination. `docs/patterns.md § Pattern 26: Socratic Prompting` gains `### Structural enforcement (STE-237)` sub-section pinning the B-side / C-side / source-probe / audit / behavioral-fixture matrix and cross-linking the magpie incident gist as the originating signal. All four in-scope skill bodies (`setup`, `brainstorm`, `spec-write`, `report-issue`) gain a `Socratic Loop Contract (STE-237)` rule block citing `AskUserQuestion` + protocol path. Test coverage: 10 unit tests on `socratic_first_turn.ts` (six-case matrix + edge cases), 9 collocated tests on `audit_log` `loop_entered:` (round-trip + permutations + back-compat), 7 fixture tests on the new probe (variants a–e + HTML-comment + multi-skill aggregation). (STE-237)
- **STE-238 — Capability-row instrumentation: literal-token MUST-emit directives + `closing_summary_capability_keys` probe.** `/spec-write` SKILL.md prose strengthened with explicit `MUST emit \`<key>\`` directives (literal backticked tokens, not paraphrased) at four emission sites: § 0b step 4 + § 4 (draft gate ⇒ `spec_write_draft_default_applied`), § 7a (commit gate ⇒ `spec_write_commit_default_applied`), § 4 (branch gate ⇒ all six `branch_gate_*` outcomes incl. new `branch_gate_skipped_already_non_main`), § 0b spec-research seed (⇒ exactly one of `spec_research_invoked` / `spec_research_no_matches` / `spec_research_shape_violation`). New static-map entry `branch_gate_skipped_already_non_main` added to `/spec-write` § 7's plain-language map with rendered prose `gate skipped — operator already off-trunk on <branch>; commit landing here per branch-isolation preference (no new branch created)`. New `/gate-check` probe #44 `closing_summary_capability_keys` (severity: error) at `adapters/_shared/src/closing_summary_capability_keys.ts` globs `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/{spec-write,gate-check,smoke-test}/SKILL.md` + `.claude/skills/{spec-write,gate-check,smoke-test}/SKILL.md`; for every key in the canonical static map, asserts the owner skill body carries a literal `MUST emit \`<key>\`` directive (regex match — backticks required; paraphrase like "the closing summary will mention <key>" does NOT satisfy). New `/smoke-test` Phase 9 — Capability-Row Emission Verification — runs three lenient-assertion fixtures (per STE-231 AC.3 shape): marker-driven draft+commit gates expect `spec_write_draft_default_applied` AND `_commit_default_applied`; marker-driven branch gate (main / off-trunk) expects `branch_gate_default_applied` / `branch_gate_skipped_already_non_main`; spec-research (project with archived FR / fresh project) expects `spec_research_invoked` / `_no_matches`. Hard-fails on missing tokens; fixture artifacts under `tests/fixtures/capability-rows/`. New pure-rendering helper `renderProbeSkipReason(...)` at `adapters/_shared/src/tracker_probe_skip_reason.ts` produces vendor-neutral cause-named skip-reason text for tracker-MCP-dependent probes; unit-tested to forbid the F9 LLM-paraphrase substring `"require Linear MCP"` across every cause; `/gate-check` probe #26 SKILL.md prose updated to cite the helper. `/smoke-test` sub-fixture 3c carries explicit `probe #37` annotation pinning the `cross-cutting-spec-stale-file-refs` probe number to prevent future doc-drift recurrence (F8 closure). Per `project_no_users_yet`, no migration shim for legacy closing summaries that lack the literal tokens — they're regenerated on next `/spec-write` invocation under the new directives. AC-STE-238.8 spec-deviation ambiguity (FR named probe #37; F9 source signal pointed at probe #26) resolved provisionally with a vendor-neutral helper applicable to any tracker-MCP-dependent probe. Test coverage: 13 unit tests on `tracker_probe_skip_reason.ts` (forbidden-substring assertion across all causes + cause-specific prose), 4 fixture tests on the new probe (variants a/b/b'/paraphrase). (STE-238)

Total test count at release: 620 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.16.0] — 2026-05-07 — "Sentinel"

M65 closes the autonomous-mode contract on the refusal side. STE-226 (M59) gave the toolkit a byte-checkable marker for default-apply; the dual was missing — when no marker is present and no live human can answer, every `requires-input:` step must refuse with NFR-10 canonical shape rather than silently model-imputing. Triggered by the v2.13.0 / 2026-05-06 incident gist where `/setup` step 7b model-imputed `tracker_mode=none` despite the skill text literally saying "Auto Mode does NOT relax `requires-input`". Single-FR milestone — the four deliverables (canonical doc + shared helper + audit-row extension + `/gate-check` probe + `/smoke-test` lockstep) are tightly coupled and ship as a unit.

### Added

- **STE-232 — Cross-skill auto-mode refusal protocol + audit `imputed` column.** New canonical doc `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/docs/auto-mode-protocol.md` with the five-section contract every gated skill cites instead of redefining the rule (`## The Rule` — harness no-questions reminder is not an override; `## Default-Apply Mechanism` — STE-226 marker; `## Refusal Mechanism` — NFR-10 shape + sentinel-still-placeholder check; `## Audit Trail` — `imputed: true|false` column with source→derived mapping table; `## Skills In Scope` — six-skill scope table). New pure-I/O helper `requireOrRefuse(spec, key, sentinel)` at `adapters/_shared/src/requires_input.ts` consolidates the four-outcome decision (user-supplied / pre-baked / default-applied / refused) driven by pre-bake flag presence, marker presence, and sentinel-still-placeholder. Throws `RequiresInputRefusedError` (NFR-10 shape carrying Verdict / Remedy / Context lines + structured `skillName` / `stepName` / `key` / `markerPresent` fields). Decision precedence is user-supplied > pre-baked > default-applied > refused; `requires-input:` steps pass `defaultValue: undefined` so the marker can never default-apply them. `## /setup audit` row format gains `imputed: true|false` via new helper `appendAuditRow(...)` at `adapters/_shared/src/setup/audit_log.ts` accepting `source: 'user-supplied' | 'pre-baked' | 'default-applied' | 'model-imputed'` and deriving `imputed = source !== 'user-supplied'`; new `parseAuditRow(line)` companion is tolerant of legacy rows (no `imputed:` column → `imputed: undefined`); `appendAuditEntry` retained as a backwards-compat wrapper deriving source from the legacy `reason` argument. New `/gate-check` probe #42 `requires_input_sentinel_coverage` (severity: error) at `adapters/_shared/src/requires_input_sentinel_coverage.ts` globs `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/*/SKILL.md` and `.claude/skills/*/SKILL.md` (matching probe #38's scope); for every skill body carrying a non-comment `requires-input:` annotation, asserts (a) a `requireOrRefuse(...)` reference AND (b) a relative-path citation of `docs/auto-mode-protocol.md`. Each missing check surfaces as a separate violation in `file:line — reason` shape. HTML-comment-scoped mentions are stripped before scanning. `/setup` step 7b refactored as the regression anchor (success path byte-identical to v2.15.0; refusal path routed through the helper). `/smoke-test` Phase 0 acceptance gate documents the three-branch resolution: marker present ⇒ default-apply; marker absent + non-interactive stdin ⇒ refuse with NFR-10; interactive ⇒ prompt. Phase 2 heredoc-injected `<dpt:auto-approve>v1</dpt:auto-approve>` body line is documented as the canonical pre-authorization mechanism in the protocol doc (STE-226 cross-reference). Test coverage: 11 unit tests on `requires_input.ts` (four-outcome matrix + NFR-10 message shape + structured error fields), 7 collocated + 10 in tests/ on `audit_log` (per-source rendering + round-trip + legacy tolerant parse), 9 on the new probe (compliant / non-compliant / vacuous / HTML-comment / dual-violation / both-surface-paths). Per `project_no_users_yet` no backward-compat shim for the audit-row format. (STE-232)

Total test count at release: 2027 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.15.0] — 2026-05-06 — "Tripwire"

M64 ships a single FR (STE-231) that extends `/smoke-test` Phase 2.X with four new runtime-regression fixture groups for the M58 / M60 / M61 / M63 cohort. Group 4 (STE-227) drives `--no-tech` end-to-end (4-step refusal/clear/completion/archive pass on Linear + Jira). Group 5 (STE-228) pins both directions of the universal branch-gate marker contract (5a marker-present, 5b marker-absent prose-only — anti-probe-collision per fixture 1b precedent). Group 6 (STE-230) asserts the spec-research subagent fired in the canonical-chain `/spec-write` log via lenient OR over the three audit rows. Group 7 (STE-225) asserts the TDD orchestrator emitted ≥ 3 `tdd-result` fenced blocks in the canonical-chain `/implement` log. Project-local `.claude/skills/smoke-test/SKILL.md` only — no plugin surface change, no new gate-check probe (per AC-STE-231.8). Original release target v2.14.0 collided with M63's same-day ship; `/implement` Phase 4 deviation shifted to v2.15.0.

### Added

- **STE-231 — Phase 2.X runtime fixtures for M58/M60/M61/M63 cohort.** New fixture groups 4 (STE-227 `--no-tech` end-to-end), 5 (STE-228 branch-gate marker contract), 6 (STE-230 spec-research subagent runtime), 7 (STE-225 TDD orchestrator forks runtime) added to `.claude/skills/smoke-test/SKILL.md` between the existing Phase 2.X summary-line section and the Phase 3 — Capture section. Group 4 is two sub-fixtures (4a Linear, 4b Jira), each driving the 4-step pass: `/spec-write --no-tech` creates flagged FR → `/implement <id>` refuses with `implement_refused_needs_technical_review` capability row → `/spec-write <id>` (no flag) clears the flag → `/implement <id>` proceeds → archival lands. Steps spawn fresh `claude -p` children using the existing heredoc-on-stdin pattern (§ STE-185) with the `<dpt:auto-approve>v1</dpt:auto-approve>` marker; per-step stdout captured to `/tmp/dpt-smoke-<tracker>-no-tech-step-<N>.log`. Group 5 is two sub-fixtures: 5a (marker present) reuses the existing canonical-chain `/spec-write` log and asserts `branch_gate_default_applied` row + `git branch --show-current` ≠ main; 5b (marker absent) spawns a marker-stripped `/spec-write` child described in prose (NOT as a fenced reference snippet — anti-probe-collision per the M59 `auto_approve_marker_in_canonical_spawns` probe scope, same technique as STE-226 fixture 1b) and asserts the inverse (no row, no branch on disk, stdout halts at gate prompt). A coverage-gap note inside group 5 documents that per-skill expansion to `/spec-archive` and `/ship-milestone` is deferred — both are explicitly NOT in the canonical chain (would corrupt real data); the canonical chain transitively exercises STE-228's branch gate for `/setup` (Phase 1 bootstrap), `/spec-write` (Phase 2 step 2), and `/implement` (Phase 2 step 3) — three of five commit-producing skills. Group 6 is a single sub-fixture against the existing `/spec-write` log; lenient OR over `spec_research_invoked` / `spec_research_no_matches` / `spec_research_shape_violation` covers every defined post-condition without over-constraining the smoke. Group 7 is a single sub-fixture against the existing `/implement` log; double-backtick code span containing the literal triple-backtick fence-tag is the assertion shape (`grep -c '^```tdd-result$' /tmp/...implement.log` ≥ 3); one fenced block per orchestrator phase (test-writer → implementer → refactorer); diagnostic carries an observed-count enumeration plus a git-log excerpt per the STE-222 group 3 precedent. Diagnostic shape `STE-<sut> runtime regression: <fixture-name>` preserved across all four groups (sut ∈ {227, 228, 230, 225}, never 231) — the diagnostic names the system-under-test, not the test infrastructure carrying the fixture (same convention as STE-220 / STE-221 / STE-222). Phase 2.X summary line section extended: existing `M56 runtime checks: PASS (...)` line preserved unchanged per AC-STE-231.6; each new group's footer paragraph contributes one of the four new per-FR runtime-check lines (`STE-227 | STE-228 | STE-230 | STE-225 runtime check: PASS|FAIL`). No new `/gate-check` probe (Phase 2.X lives in project-local SKILL.md; `/gate-check` scans plugin-internal SKILL.md files only). Capability-key map untouched — every greped row is pre-existing. AC-STE-231.9 (live `/conformance-loop` archival evidence) ships `[~]` deferred per memory `feedback_smoke_post_ship_retroactive`. AC-STE-231.10 documents out-of-scope assertions (`/report-issue` not added; `/spec-archive` + `/ship-milestone` per-skill expansion deferred). (STE-231)

Total test count at release: 1989 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.14.0] — 2026-05-06 — "Precedent"

M63 ships a single FR (STE-230) — a topic-aware retrieval primitive that lets `/brainstorm` and `/spec-write` pull *targeted* context from prior FRs (active + archived) without polluting the parent skill's context window. New `/dev-process-toolkit:spec-research` forked skill (`context: fork`, `user-invocable: false`) pairs with a Read-only Haiku subagent (`spec-researcher`, `tools: Read, Grep, Glob`); the subagent scans `specs/frs/**` and emits a fixed-shape ≤ 25-line block (banner + Related FRs / Prior Decisions / Reusable ACs sections). Industry SDD tooling (GitHub Spec Kit, OpenSpec) addresses the same problem via a project-level `constitution` doc or by lifting deltas into living specs at archive time; M63 takes a third path — on-demand topic-aware retrieval via a context-isolated subagent, no schema churn, no new artifact, archive stays a passive audit trail.

### Added

- **STE-230 — `spec-research` subagent for context retrieval in `/brainstorm` and `/spec-write`.** New `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/agents/spec-researcher.md` (Read-only Haiku, `tools: Read, Grep, Glob`) paired with new `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/spec-research/SKILL.md` (`context: fork`, `agent: spec-researcher`, `user-invocable: false`, `argument-hint: '<topic description>'`) — a context-isolated retrieval primitive. Given a topic, the subagent globs `specs/frs/*.md` (active) and `specs/frs/archive/*.md` (history), selects the top ≤ 3 candidates by relevance, and emits a fixed-shape block: literal banner line `> [historical reference — decisions below may be stale; use as background, not authority]` immediately above a fenced ` ```spec-research-result ` block with exactly three `## ` sections in canonical order (`## Related FRs`, `## Prior Decisions`, `## Reusable ACs / Patterns`); ≤ 25 lines total; empty fallback uses `- (none found)` placeholder bullets; truncation marker `- (… <K> more truncated)` appended on overflow. `/spec-write` § 0b inserts a Spec-research seed sub-paragraph between step 2 ("Build canonical frontmatter") and step 3 ("AC prefix") that calls `/dev-process-toolkit:spec-research <topic>` (FR title + 1-line summary); the returned block seeds the subsequent `## Technical Design` interview. `/brainstorm` adds § 1.5 between Step 1 (Clarify the Problem) and Step 2 (Explore Approaches) that calls `/dev-process-toolkit:spec-research <topic>` with the clarified problem statement; Step 2's proposed approaches reference returned precedents alongside the model's own analysis. Both invocations skip under `--no-tech` (vacuous: technical-design interview / Step 2 are themselves skipped, no consumer for the seed). Branch-gate exemption via `NON_COMMIT_PRODUCING_SKILLS` allowlist append in `adapters/_shared/src/commit_producing_skill_branch_gate.ts` — `spec-research` joins `report-issue` as a read-side / outbound-only flow exempt from STE-228's `commit_producing_skill_branch_gate` probe. Three new capability keys (`spec_research_invoked` / `spec_research_no_matches` / `spec_research_shape_violation`) in `/spec-write` § 7 static plain-language map (rendered as a single compound row matching the `report_issue_*` precedent for NFR-1 length-cap fit). New `/gate-check` probe #41 `spec_research_result_shape` (severity: error) at `adapters/_shared/src/spec_research_result_shape.ts` walks recorded `.dpt-locks/**/spec-research-result.txt` logs and asserts (a) banner line on the line immediately above the opening fence, (b) fence opens with `\`\`\`spec-research-result`, (c) exactly three `## ` headings inside the fence in canonical order, (d) entire block ≤ 25 lines (banner + opening fence + sections + closing fence). Vacuous when no result log is recorded — the common no-invocation path. AC-STE-230.13 smoke covers six cases: two-match populated block, zero-match empty fallback, > 3 truncation marker, read-only invariant, `/spec-write --no-tech` short-circuits the call, marker-driven `/brainstorm` step 1.5 fires at the documented boundary. Plan AC #3 (live `/brainstorm` or `/spec-write` invocation observed firing the insertion) ships `[~]` deferred per memory `feedback_smoke_post_ship_retroactive` — operator-observed verification on the next live `/brainstorm` or `/spec-write --tech` run. The original `## Cautions` section in the output contract was dropped on user feedback during the brainstorm session: gate-probing contradiction detection is shape-not-content; the "may be stale" banner is the deterministic hint, the parent LLM owns the apply-or-diverge call. Wiring into `/spec-review` and `/implement` Phase 1 was discussed and explicitly rejected — the agent only feeds `/brainstorm` and `/spec-write`. (STE-230)

Total test count at release: 1989 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.13.0] — 2026-05-06 — "Guardrail"

M61 + M62 ship together — both add deterministic gates against silent leaks. M61 (STE-228) lifts `/implement`'s branch-proposal helper into a shared pre-commit gate that every commit-producing skill calls before staging; the trunk-OK allowlist narrows from `[chore, docs, ci]` to `[ci]` only, so protected-trunk repos can no longer accidentally land `chore(specs):` or `docs(specs):` commits on `main` and discover the rejection at push time. M62 (STE-229) ships `/dev-process-toolkit:report-issue` — privacy-first incident-report capture with seven-pattern secret redaction, a preview gate, and a secret-gist publish step that hands the URL back for triage or self-debug via `/brainstorm <gist-url>`. Both milestones favor structural enforcement (an explicit gate, an explicit redaction pass, an explicit allowlist) over instructional prose.

### Added

- **STE-228 — Universal pre-commit branch gate; trunk-OK narrowed to `ci`.** Every commit-producing skill (`/setup`, `/spec-write`, `/spec-archive`, `/ship-milestone`, `/implement`) calls a shared `requireCommittableBranch({ commitType, proposedBranchName, currentBranch, isAutoMode })` gate from `adapters/_shared/src/require_committable_branch.ts` before staging. The gate refuses to commit on `main` / `master` unless `commitType ∈ TRUNK_OK_TYPES = ["ci"]` — `chore` and `docs` no longer ship directly to trunk (supersedes STE-202 AC-STE-202.5; behavior break is intentional and unmitigated per `project_no_users_yet`). Each skill carries a `branchNameFor(...)` builder under `skills/<skill>/branch_name_for.ts` that maps the operation to a canonical branch shape (e.g., `feat/<id>-<slug>` for `/implement`, `release/v<X.Y.Z>` for `/ship-milestone`, `chore/setup-bootstrap` for `/setup`, `chore/archive-<scope>` for `/spec-archive`, `docs/specs-cross-cutting` for `/spec-write` cross-cutting). Concurrent runs of literal-named skills coexist via collision-suffix probe (`-2`, `-3`, …). New `/gate-check` probe `commit_producing_skill_branch_gate` (severity: error) globs each commit-producing skill's SKILL.md and refuses any `git commit` reference not preceded in document order by a documented call to `requireCommittableBranch`. Off-trunk runs are a silent no-op (the existing `feedback_branch_isolation` memory rule composes cleanly). Auto-mode default-apply uses the M59 `<dpt:auto-approve>v1</dpt:auto-approve>` marker. The `/implement` Phase 0.b″ trunk-OK list narrows from `[chore, docs, ci]` to `[ci]` at the same call-site (STE-228 supersedes STE-202 AC-STE-202.5). (STE-228)

- **STE-229 — `/report-issue` skill: structured bug-report capture.** New `/dev-process-toolkit:report-issue` ships a privacy-first incident-report capture: four Socratic prompts (what happened / what was expected / severity / reproducibility) collect the dev narrative, then the skill bundles plugin version, `git rev-parse HEAD`, `git status --porcelain`, `git log -10 --oneline`, last `/gate-check` log, redacted `.claude/settings.json{,.local}`, and the session's skill-invocation list into a curated payload. `--full` mode (or an in-flow `[y/N]` opt-in inside the preview gate) bundles the current session's JSONL transcript via a slug + mtime heuristic in `find_current_session.ts` (honors `CLAUDE_CONFIG_DIR` for non-default config roots such as `~/.claude-st`). Every text artifact passes through `scrubSecrets` from `adapters/_shared/src/scrub_secrets.ts` — seven canonical `SECRET_PATTERNS` (Anthropic `sk-ant-…` / OpenAI legacy + `sk-proj-…` v2 / GitHub PAT `gh[pous]_…` / AWS `AKIA…` / generic `(api_key|token|password|secret)=…` / JWT `eyJ…` / AWS secret-access-key heuristic) with longest-prefix-first ordering so `sk-ant-…` keys attribute to `anthropic_api_key` rather than `openai_api_key`. Preview gate prints file list + sizes + redaction summary, then prompts `Push to gist? [y / n / edit]`; the `<dpt:auto-approve>v1</dpt:auto-approve>` marker default-applies `y` per STE-226's contract. Publish via `gh gist create -s -d "<title>" report.md metadata.json [transcript.jsonl]`; closing summary (≥100 bytes) carries the gist URL + redaction-match counts + severity + a `Next:` block offering the `/brainstorm <gist-url>` round-trip for self-debug. New `NON_COMMIT_PRODUCING_SKILLS` allowlist in `commit_producing_skill_branch_gate.ts` documents the read-side / outbound-only exemption (`/report-issue` is on the list); the probe consults the allowlist and the disjointness invariant is test-asserted. Cross-cutting: `/brainstorm` accepts a gist URL as the first positional argument and seeds Step 1 from the `gh gist view` payload, closing the round-trip loop in two operator gestures. Three new capability rows in `/spec-write` § 7 (`report_issue_default_applied` / `report_issue_declined` / `report_issue_redacted_payload`, merged into one `report_issue_*` table row per `branch_gate_*` precedent to stay under the NFR-1 ≤300-line cap). AC-STE-229.12's smoke covers seven cases (gh-auth-fail refusal, default-mode payload shape, full-mode payload shape, redaction-with-planted-secrets, preview-gate decline, closing-summary byte-floor, marker-present auto-push); 22 unit tests on `scrubSecrets` (every pattern, longest-prefix-first ordering, separator normalization, idempotency), 13 on `findCurrentSession` (slug derivation, mtime ordering, missing-slug, env-var resolution), 12 on doc-conformance. Plan ACs 3 + 4 (live manual `/report-issue` + `/brainstorm <gist-url>` runs) ship `[~]` deferred per plan task 8 — operator-observed verification at `/ship-milestone M62` time. (STE-229)

Total test count at release: 1938 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.12.0] — 2026-05-06 — "Handoff"

M60 lets non-technical stakeholders (PMs, product owners, operations leads) drop a draft FR into `specs/frs/` without running the full `/spec-write` interview. The new `--no-tech` flag on `/spec-write` and `/brainstorm` gates the technical-design + testing-spec interviews; the resulting FR lands with `needs_technical_review: true` in frontmatter and a canonical placeholder line in both technical sections, plus a `needs-technical-review` tracker label on Linear/Jira boards. `/implement` refuses to ship a flagged FR until a technical reviewer runs `/spec-write <FR-id>` (no flag) — auto-detected at § 0a, no special incantation; the auto-resume drops the field on save and removes the label. A new `/gate-check` probe `needs_technical_review_consistency` enforces the flag ⇔ placeholder bidirectional invariant with four distinct violation kinds (`missing_placeholder`, `stray_placeholder`, `empty_section`, `missing_section`) so missing or stale placeholder bodies fail loudly. Same FR file shape, no new artifact type, zero migration for the 200+ existing archived FRs (omission ≡ false). Architectural shift: the toolkit now carries an explicit "draft state" without introducing a new file path — the field IS the integration point, gating `/implement`, the auto-resume, the consistency probe, and the tracker board's visual signal in one frontmatter key.

### Added

- **STE-227 — `--no-tech` flag for non-technical FR drafting + `needs_technical_review` gate.** New `--no-tech` flag on `/spec-write` and `/brainstorm` skips the technical-design + testing-spec interviews on the new-FR creation path and writes the canonical placeholder line `[needs technical review — run /spec-write <FR-id> to complete]` (literal `<FR-id>` substituted with the real ID at write time) into both `## Technical Design` and `## Testing` bodies. Frontmatter carries `needs_technical_review: true` via `buildFRFrontmatter(spec, trackerBinding, { needsTechnicalReview: true })` — third optional opts param (absent ≡ false; round-trip tested). `Provider.sync(spec)` still fires; in tracker mode with label-push capability the `needs-technical-review` label is appended to `defaultLabels` (or seeded as a single-element array when absent); adapters without label-push surface the `needs_technical_review_label_unsupported` capability row. `/brainstorm --no-tech` skips Step 2 (Explore Approaches — non-technical users can't pick architectural tradeoffs) and Step 4 propagates the flag (recommends `/spec-write --no-tech`). `/spec-write <FR-id>` (no flag) auto-detects `needs_technical_review: true` at § 0a resolver entry, skips the requirement + AC interview (already filled), runs technical + testing only, and on save drops the field from frontmatter entirely + removes the `needs-technical-review` tracker label on the same `Provider.sync` call. `/implement` refuses at Phase 0.b′ resolver entry (NFR-10 canonical refusal, no claim, no branch, zero side effects) — single-FR variant names the FR + remedy `Run /spec-write <FR-id> to complete the technical design + testing sections`; milestone-scope variant enumerates every flagged active FR in M\<N> in one batch. New `/gate-check` probe #40 `needs_technical_review_consistency` (severity: error) walks `specs/frs/*.md` and asserts the flag ⇔ placeholder bidirectional invariant — em-dash-anchored substring match (`needs technical review —`) so ordinary prose mentioning the bare two-word phrase doesn't false-positive; four distinct violation kinds with independent remedy text (`missing_placeholder`, `stray_placeholder`, `empty_section`, `missing_section`). Four new capability keys in `/spec-write` § 7 static map (combined into 2 rows for NFR-1 length-cap fit) + `/implement` closing summary: `fr_needs_technical_review`, `fr_technical_review_cleared`, `needs_technical_review_label_unsupported`, `implement_refused_needs_technical_review`. Same FR file shape — same five-section skeleton, same frontmatter keys plus one optional flag; existing FRs without the field stay byte-identical. AC-STE-227.11 (smoke fixture extension covering the end-to-end pass on Linear + Jira) ships `[~]` deferred per memory `feedback_smoke_post_ship_retroactive`. (STE-227)

Total test count at release: 1797 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.11.0] — 2026-05-06 — "Deterministic"

M58 + M59 ship together — both replace prose-judgment contracts with byte-checkable deterministic mechanisms. M58 introduces a multi-agent `/dev-process-toolkit:tdd` orchestrator that runs each TDD phase in an isolated subagent context (Skills `context: fork` + custom-subagent pairing) — test-writer cannot see the implementation, implementer sees one AC at a time, refactorer runs once-at-end after all GREEN. Hand-off is a strict ` ```tdd-result ` fenced YAML block parsed deterministically; failures route through a five-mode classifier with bounded retries (max-2 semantic / single-format) before halting. M59 closes STE-220's third attempt by replacing the prose-only Auto-mode/`-p` detection contract with an explicit `<dpt:auto-approve>v1</dpt:auto-approve>` pre-authorization marker line that gates default-apply at every relevant SKILL.md gate. Two prose-only attempts (STE-213 in M55, STE-220 in M56) had been falsified across four end-to-end smoke runs; M59's marker is byte-checkable at runtime — no LLM judgment, no `<system-reminder>` introspection. The shared theme: structural enforcement over instructional prose, deterministic gates over inferred intent.

### Added

- **STE-225 — Multi-agent `/tdd` orchestrator with context isolation.** Replaces the single-context `/dev-process-toolkit:tdd` with a four-skill orchestrator (one main-context driver + three `context: fork` children) paired with three plugin-bundled subagents (`tdd-test-writer` / `tdd-implementer` / `tdd-refactorer`, each with `tools: Read, Grep, Glob, Write, Edit, Bash` allowlist + `maxTurns: 8` — `Agent` excluded so children cannot nest-spawn). Cycle granularity: test-writer once per FR with the full AC list batched, implementer once per AC, refactorer once at end. Hand-off contract: every child ends with exactly one fenced ` ```tdd-result ` YAML block parsed by `parseTddResultBlock` from `adapters/_shared/src/tdd_result.ts`. Bounded retries via `recordTddFailure` from `tdd_retry_state.ts` (max-2 per role per AC for semantic failures A/B/C/E; single targeted retry for format violation D). Halt path emits failure mode + retry count + last block (or raw output) via `formatHaltReport` from `tdd_halt_report.ts` and exits non-zero. Retry prompt **injects only raw failing-test output** — no orchestrator-side analysis — preserving the test-writer-cannot-see-implementation guarantee. `/implement` Phase 2 step 8 invokes the orchestrator inline (no separate opt-in path). New `/gate-check` probe #39 `tdd_orchestrator_integrity` (severity: error) asserts (a) the four skill paths exist, (b) children carry `context: fork`, (c) `agent:` resolves to a real agents/*.md, (d) `user-invocable: false` on children, (e) subagent `tools` excludes `Agent`. Two-tier smoke: Bun-mocked unit tests (parser / retry / batching / halt — every commit) + env-gated headless live fixture at `tests/fixtures/tdd-smoke/` (single-AC `add(a, b)` FR, gated by `DPT_TDD_LIVE_SMOKE=1`, behavioral assertions only — never exact-string). Plugin-bundled subagents drop `hooks` / `mcpServers` / `permissionMode` per Claude Code's plugin-subagent constraint; behavioral specialization comes exclusively from the SKILL.md prompt + `tools` allowlist. `docs/skill-anatomy.md` and `docs/patterns.md` updated with the four-skill TDD shape; new patterns.md section "Multi-Agent TDD Orchestrator (STE-225)" documents the load-bearing rationale. Closes Gap 1 of `research/sdd-tdd-improvements-2026-05.md` (marked DONE). Test count delta: +89 (1652 → 1741 baseline pre-release). (STE-225)

- **STE-226 — Auto-mode/`-p` carve-out: explicit pre-authorization marker.** Replaces the brittle "auto-detect Auto Mode Active in `<system-reminder>`" path with a byte-checkable marker line `<dpt:auto-approve>v1</dpt:auto-approve>`. When a parent skill spawns a child via `claude -p` and emits the marker line in the prompt body, the child's gates default-apply `y` and emit the documented audit rows (`spec_write_draft_default_applied` + `spec_write_commit_default_applied`); without the marker, gates fire interactively. The marker is detected by literal string match — no regex, no whitespace-tolerant parsing, no LLM judgment. Marker shape `<dpt:auto-approve>v1</dpt:auto-approve>` is byte-repeated across `/spec-write` SKILL.md § 0b step 4, § 4, § 7a (paste-not-paraphrase, byte-grep-checkable). Parent skills (`/smoke-test`, `/conformance-loop`) inject the marker into every documented `claude -p` reference snippet that targets a child carrying a gate. New `/gate-check` probe #38 `auto_approve_marker_in_canonical_spawns` (severity: error) globs `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/*/SKILL.md` + `.claude/skills/*/SKILL.md` for `claude -p` heredoc-on-stdin spawn fences and asserts each carries the marker line on its own line — non-prompt-bearing `< /dev/null` snippets are out of scope. Architectural lesson driving M59: instructional SKILL.md prose for the LLM is not a reliable substitute for an explicit byte-checkable contract when the LLM is processing the same prose to decide whether to apply it. Two prose-only attempts (STE-213 in M55, STE-220 in M56) were falsified across four end-to-end smoke runs (2026-05-04 v2.8.0 Linear F2-1 + Jira C-F1; 2026-05-05 v2.10.0 `/conformance-loop` iter-1 F1 + M1). The legacy `Auto Mode Active` system-reminder detection path is removed; marker is the single deterministic mechanism. No backward-compatibility shim per `project_no_users_yet`. AC-STE-226.6 (real `-p` stdout in archival Notes) ships `[~]` deferred per memory `feedback_smoke_post_ship_retroactive`. (STE-226)

Total test count at release: 1741 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.10.0] — 2026-05-05 — "Convergence"

M57 ships the `/conformance-loop` project-local skill — a parent-driven wrapper that runs `/smoke-test` against both Linear and Jira trackers in parallel each iteration, aggregates the per-tracker findings files into one cross-tracker-deduplicated report, and (in opt-in `--auto-fix` mode) sequentially dispatches `/spec-write` + `/implement` per high-severity finding until the loop terminates on `green`, `max-iterations`, or `no-progress`. Default `capture-only` mode preserves `/smoke-test`'s "Capture, don't fix" rule unchanged for raw invocations; `--auto-fix` is the formally-sanctioned exception under explicit safety rails (`--max-iterations` cap, no-progress detection, high-severity-only filter that excludes driver-side caveats by construction). The skill is project-local (`.claude/skills/conformance-loop/SKILL.md`) — downstream plugin users never see it, the override is scoped to the dogfooded toolkit repo only. Replaces the manual two-terminal smoke workflow with one invocation; post-M55/M56 manual triage of 6/3+ FRs per cycle motivated the automation.

### Added

- **STE-224 — `/conformance-loop` skill: automated test+fix loop wrapping `/smoke-test`.** Adds `.claude/skills/conformance-loop/SKILL.md` (project-local, `disable-model-invocation: true`). Argument parsing: `--auto-fix` (default OFF — capture-only is the default), `--max-iterations N` (default 3), `--linear-team STE`, `--jira-project KEY` (required when Jira child fires), `--dry-run` (test-only mock for `conformance-loop-dry-run.test.ts`). Five pre-flight refusals (a)–(e) — toolkit-repo cwd, `/smoke-test` skill present, Linear MCP+team (delegates to `/smoke-test` #3+#5), Atlassian MCP+project (delegates to `/smoke-test` #7+#8), both `../dpt-test-project-{linear,jira}` paths free (delegates to `/smoke-test` #2). Phase 0 pre-approval gate prints both-trackers contract + `max-iterations × ~10 min × 2`-tracker wall-clock estimate; Auto Mode / `claude -p` default-apply per the canonical detection contract. Phase A backgrounds two `claude -p /smoke-test` subprocess calls via Bash heredoc + `wait`, fail-fast on either non-zero RC; aggregator parses the canonical `/tmp/dpt-smoke-findings-<date>-{linear,jira}.md` files into `/tmp/dpt-conformance-loop-<date>-iter-<N>.md` with two-pass cross-tracker dedup (exact-match on `STE-<N> runtime regression: <fixture>` then ≥80% normalized-body substring overlap with `~probable-dup` flag for operator review). Phase B sequentially walks high-severity findings — per finding spawns `claude -p /dev-process-toolkit:spec-write` (collision-resistant `EOF_TAG="PROMPT_EOF_$(uuidgen)"` heredoc delimiter), captures the freshly-allocated tracker ID with a `[ -z "${NEW_TRACKER_ID}" ]` fail-fast guard, then spawns `claude -p /dev-process-toolkit:implement <id>`. Three new capability keys for closing-summary rendering: `conformance_loop_terminated_green`, `conformance_loop_terminated_exhausted`, `conformance_loop_terminated_no_progress`. Threat-model section documents the deliberate override of `/smoke-test`'s "Capture, don't fix" + "One run per release cycle" rules with safety rails enumerated (max-iterations cap, capture-only default, no-progress detection, high-severity-only filter); cross-reference paragraph added to `/smoke-test` SKILL.md naming `/conformance-loop` as the formally-sanctioned auto-fix exception path. Path-safety guard delegated to each `/smoke-test` child's pre-flight #6 (the `realpath`-based allow-list check fires before `bypassPermissions` activates in the child layer; parent does not duplicate). Test coverage: 4 new doc-conformance test files (`conformance-loop-{args,aggregator,termination,dry-run}.test.ts`) — 34 tests total, doc-conformance pattern matching `smoke-test-driver-hardening.test.ts`. AC-STE-224.4 and AC-STE-224.5 manual-smoke ACs ship `[~]` deferred per memory `feedback_smoke_post_ship_retroactive` — captured `/conformance-loop --max-iterations 1` stdout against live Linear + Jira MCPs targets the next 2026-05-* smoke run as external evidence. (STE-224)

Total test count at release: 1639 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

Clean tree → no advisory. The literal `tree dirty:` token is machine-greppable for the smoke driver. Auto-commit was rejected per CLAUDE.md core principle "human approval before commit"; the advisory is informational and `/simplify` continues to exit 0. Total recognizer (every input returns boolean, never throws). Patterns documented inline in `skills/gate-check/SKILL.md` § probe #28. Closes 2026-05-04 Linear smoke #10 F4 — verify lines that deliberately reference deleted paths to assert their absence stop false-positive-flagging. (STE-217)

## [2.7.0] — 2026-05-04 — "Roundtrip"

Smoke #11 follow-up milestone. Closes 26 verified bugs from the 2026-05-04 Dart-lib smoke run on `dpt_test_lib` + the 2026-05-04 Flutter-app smoke run on `dpt_test_lib2` — 9 FRs across plan-file hygiene, milestone-attach capability split, tracker availability + Auto Mode `requires-input` enforcement, scaffolding-milestone closure, ship-milestone task-bullet pre-flight, doc/workflow polish, setup-time canonical-shape hygiene, Phase 4 archival hardening, and Linear AC-token round-trip preservation. Five new `/gate-check` probes lock the regressions in place. AC-STE-195.5 retroactive validation carries forward to M55 (no real stream-idle surfaced during M54).

### Added

- **STE-197 — Plan-file hygiene: trimmed template + YAML frontmatter + bootstrap allocation rules.** `templates/spec-templates/plan.md.template` rewritten — single `## M<N>:` section, `---` YAML frontmatter (5 fields: `milestone`, `status`, `archived_at`, `kickoff_branch`, `frozen_at`), no `## Milestone Dependency Graph`. `/setup` step 8 marks bootstrap milestones with `kind: scaffolding` + a single `<scaffolding>` FR row (no `Provider.sync`, no `<tracker-id>` literal). `/implement` Phase 4 prose handles legacy frontmatter-less plans by prepending one. New `/gate-check` probe `plan-file-single-milestone` (#32) flags multi-milestone plan files at ADVISORY. (STE-197)
- **STE-198 — Milestone-attach: auto-create branch + capability key split.** `attach_project_milestone.ts` returns `{ capability, createdName? }`; the `supports("project_milestone")` check short-circuits on adapters that opt out. Capability map split: `milestone_attach_skipped_adapter_limit` (renamed from `milestone_attach_unavailable`, deprecated alias retained one minor-version cycle) + new `milestone_create_required` for the auto-create branch. Linear projects with zero milestones now auto-create the milestone via `mcp__linear__save_milestone` (same authorization scope as the prior `save_issue`, no extra prompt). (STE-198)
- **STE-199 — Tracker availability + Auto Mode requires-input.** `/setup` step 7b grows three branches beyond NFR-10 refusal: first-run-deferral writes `team: <deferred>` / `project: <deferred>` + `workspace_binding_deferred` capability row; `--resume-tracker-binding` flag fills the binding after operator authenticates; sentinel-returning resolver refuses Auto Mode runs without a `--tracker=<mode>` pre-bake (`requires_input_refused` row). `/implement` Phase 1 step 0.a pre-flight probe enumerates `mcp__<tracker>__*` tools; missing-tools refuses unless `--code-only` flag is set (skips Phase 1 0.c/0.e/0.f tracker writes + Phase 4d release transition; surfaces `tracker_skipped` rows). `--tracker=<mode>` documented as a first-class `/setup` argument. (STE-199)
- **STE-200 — Scaffolding-milestone closure.** `/spec-archive M<N>` auto-detects plan-only branch when FR set is empty AND plan carries `kind: scaffolding` OR all task checkboxes are `[x]`/`[deferred]`. `--plan-only` flag forces the branch. `/implement` Phase 1 slim-closure detects zero claimable FRs + all-checked plan and routes through `/spec-archive M<N>` plan-only. Phase 5 silent-skip extends to zero-FR / `kind: scaffolding` milestones. New capability key `plan_only_archival`. New helper `evaluatePlanOnlyEligibility` in `adapters/_shared/src/plan_only_archival.ts`. (STE-200)
- **STE-201 — `/ship-milestone` pre-flight walks `**Tasks:**` block.** Refusal #1 now walks the `**Tasks:**` checklist in addition to the FR-row table; tasks unbacked by an FR row (or with `status: active` backing) refuse via the AC-STE-201.2 NFR-10 shape naming `<count>` unbacked tasks. `[deferred]` marker explicitly recognized as ship-OK. New `/gate-check` probe `plan-task-fr-coverage` (#33, ADVISORY) flags the same divergence on active plans. (STE-201)
- **STE-209 — Setup-time canonical-shape hygiene.** `templates/permissions.json` rewritten: explicit-subcommand allowlist replaces `Bash(<cmd> *)` globs (the harness denies any glob-shaped Bash rule when `/setup` writes `.claude/settings.json` on a fresh repo). `docs/setup-tracker-mode.md` MCP entry shape corrected to `{"type": "http", "url": "..."}` (was `{"transport": "streamable-http", ...}` — `/doctor` rejects). `/setup` step 1b doctor probe now reads the per-stack invocation prefix from `examples/<stack>/gate-commands.md` (`fvm flutter` when declared; bare `flutter` otherwise). New helper `doctorInvocationFor`. New `/gate-check` probes `mcp-config-shape` (#34, ERROR for toolkit templates / ADVISORY for user `.mcp.json`) + `setup-permissions-shape` (#35, ADVISORY). Backwards-compat: existing user files untouched; drift surfaces only in probes. (STE-209)
- **STE-210 — Phase 4 archival hardening.** `/ship-milestone` Step 1 grows an `archive/` fallback (reads from `specs/plan/archive/M<N>.md` when active path is missing AND every FR row is `status: archived`; refuses with NFR-10 on mixed-status). `/implement` Phase 4 archival reorder: `git mv` → frontmatter flip at archive path → `git add` (the previous order staged the rename with un-flipped index content). New helper `archiveFRWithFlip(repoRoot, frPath, archivedAt) → archivePath` wraps the post-`git mv` flip. New `/gate-check` probe `archive-frontmatter-coherent` (#36, ERROR) asserts archived files carry `status: archived` + non-null `archived_at:`. Fixed the F11 staging-order bug shipped in this very milestone's archival flow. (STE-210)
- **STE-211 — Linear AC-token round-trip preservation.** New `formatLinearDescription` (Linear adapter, `adapters/linear/src/format_description.ts`) wraps AC prefixes in inline-code fences before push (`AC-STE-NNN.N` → `` AC-`STE-NNN`.N ``); Linear's auto-linker treats backticked tokens as literal code and skips them. New `stripLinearACFences` strips both backticks AND legacy `<issue id="...">STE-NNN</issue>.N` XML wrappers on import — targeted by the AC-prefix shape so bare issue references in prose stay auto-linked. `importFromTracker` calls the strip helper for the Linear adapter. `/spec-write`'s AC-list diff/resolve loop normalizes both sides to plain shape before comparing, eliminating spurious "remote modified" diffs. Round-trip property: `strip(format(x)) === x`. Backwards-compat: existing mangled descriptions converge on next push. (STE-211)

### Changed

- **STE-202 — Doc & workflow polish (5 mechanical edits).** `templates/CLAUDE.md.template` Workflows block lists `/simplify` in the Feature row. `specs/plan.md` (singular) references in `/implement` SKILL.md replaced with `specs/plan/<M#>.md`. `adapters/_shared/src/resolve.ts` adds `milestone` as a first-class resolver kind (`^M\d+$`), routed before tracker-ID detection; `/implement` Phase 1 step 0.b' references it directly. `templates/CLAUDE.md.template` `## Task Tracking` documents the `branch_template:` trunk-OK allowlist (`chore`, `docs`, `ci` permitted on trunk; `feat`, `fix`, `refactor`, `perf` enforce derived branch). `/setup` step 7d emits a new `docs_default_applied` capability row in the closing summary when autonomous mode applies the all-false default. (AC-STE-202.4 superseded by STE-209's AC.1/AC.2.) (STE-202)

Total test count at release: 1516 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.6.0] — 2026-05-04 — "Sensitivity"

Smoke #10 follow-up milestone (3 FRs from the 2026-05-04 Linear + Jira smoke runs against v2.5.0). Calibrates `/gate-check` probe #26 to respect `/spec-write`'s capability-gap declaration channel — Linear smoke runs no longer false-positive-fail on missing project milestones. Builds in stream-idle retry-with-rollback for `/smoke-test` Phase 2 prompt-bearing child spawns, turning a known Anthropic-API transient into a quiet retry. Closes the four-run-old `/simplify` no-op-gate-skip documentation gap.

### Added

- **STE-194 — `/gate-check` probe #26 advisory on capability-gap declaration.** Probe #26 (`tracker-project-milestone-attached`) now reads each FR's `## Notes` body for the word-bounded `milestone_attach_unavailable` token (the canonical capability key `/spec-write` emits per its Step 7 map). Token + null binding routes the missing-binding outcome to ADVISORY (severity = note, NOT GATE FAILED) with the canonical prose `milestone-attach skipped — capability gap declared in FR Notes (milestone_attach_unavailable)`. Mismatched bindings still hard-fail — the token only excuses absence, not divergence. Closes the smoke-driver false-positive surface where Linear-mode runs created tickets in projects with zero milestones by construction. (STE-194)
- **STE-196 — `/simplify` SKILL.md no-op carve-out section.** Adds `## When this is a no-op {#when-this-is-a-no-op}` to `/simplify`'s SKILL.md naming both preconditions (working tree clean + prior `/gate-check` returned clean) and the rationale (re-running an unchanged tree against an already-clean gate produces no signal change → save tokens). Verify step + Rules section cross-link the new heading by name. Closes the four-run-old smoke gap (#6, #7, #8, #9). (STE-196)

### Changed

- **STE-195 — `/smoke-test` stream-idle retry-with-rollback for prompt-bearing children.** `/smoke-test` Phase 2 prompt-bearing spawns (`/setup`, `/spec-write`, `/implement`) gain a documented retry-with-rollback sub-flow on the `API Error: Stream idle timeout` Anthropic-API transient. One retry after `git clean -fdq -e .claude -e .mcp.json && git checkout -- .` in the test project's cwd; double-timeout aborts via NFR-10 canonical refusal naming both attempt timestamps + the recipe. AC-STE-195.5 (manual chain validation) ships `[~]` per smoke retroactive-validation framing — non-deterministic failure mode. (STE-195)

## [2.5.0] — 2026-05-02 — "Heredoc"

Smoke #9 / Jira-run-2 follow-up (7 FRs from the 2026-05-01 Linear + Jira smoke runs against v2.4.0). Retires the `/tmp/dpt-smoke-prompt-*.txt` path entirely — heredoc-on-stdin replaces the file-on-disk prompt-delivery surface and closes the cross-tracker content-swap window that triggered the Jira-run-2 corruption recovery (the fourth escalation in the stale-`/tmp` family). Hardens the smoke driver across Phase 0.5 (cleanup glob widening), Phase 1 (Linear project-name auto-disambiguation), Phase 2 (`< /dev/null` discipline for non-prompt children + heredoc partition), and pre-flight #8 (single-hit name-match KEY surfacing). Tightens `/setup`'s scaffold-deliverable boundary so restrictive driver prompts can't license skips. Adds explicit ADF-escape-tolerance tests for the Jira `pull_acs` description-body parser (new canonical pull_acs module + 9 unit cases including indented-`##` boundary).

### Added

- **STE-187 — Auto-disambiguate same-day Linear project names.** `/smoke-test` Phase 1 Linear-path now lists existing projects by name before `save_project`; on collision, appends `-v<N>` where N is the smallest unused integer ≥ 2. Deterministic, inspectable, audit-trail-friendly. Worked example: smoke #8 → `(2026-05-01)`, smoke #9 same day → `(2026-05-01-v2)`. Closes the manual `-v2` workaround surfaced by the 2026-05-01 Linear smoke. (STE-187)
- **STE-190 — Jira `pull_acs` ADF-escape tolerance tests + canonical parser module.** New `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/adapters/_shared/src/jira_pull_acs.ts` exposes `parseJiraDescriptionAcs(body) → AC[]` for the description-body path; tolerates `[x]`/`[ ]` and ADF-escaped `\[x\]`/`\[ \]` round-trip forms by design. Co-located test file ships 9 cases covering canonical, ADF-escaped, section-boundary (including indented-`##`), and absent-section variants. `adapters/jira.md` § `pull_acs` now documents the ADF round-trip artifact and the failure mode if tolerance were dropped. (STE-190)

### Changed

- **STE-185 — Heredoc-on-stdin first-class; retire `/tmp/dpt-smoke-prompt-*.txt`.** `/smoke-test` Phase 2 prompt-bearing children (`/setup`, `/spec-write`, `/implement`) now receive their prompt body via single-quoted bash heredoc on stdin; the parent no longer writes prompt files to disk. Threat-model paragraph names the linter / external-process content-swap attack surface (Jira-run-2 F1: an external linter swapped a Jira-flavored prompt with a stale Linear-flavored stub mid-run, causing silent cross-tracker corruption); heredoc closes the window. Phase 0.5 `rm -f /tmp/dpt-smoke-prompt-*.txt` is retained as defense-in-depth against pre-STE-185 driver versions during transition; expected to be a no-op on post-STE-185 runs. (STE-185)
- **STE-186 — Phase 0.5 cleanup glob widens to `/tmp/dpt-smoke-mcp-config-*.json`.** Single regex covers both `linear` and `jira` variants. Audit-trail invariant explicitly documented: the findings file (`/tmp/dpt-smoke-findings-<date>-<tracker>.md`) and the approval record (`/tmp/dpt-smoke-<date>-<tracker>-approval.txt`) stay across runs and are never widened into the cleanup set. (STE-186)
- **STE-188 — `< /dev/null` for non-prompt Phase 2 child spawns.** `/spec-review`, `/simplify`, and `/gate-check` snippets pipe `< /dev/null` immediately before the log redirect to silence `claude -p`'s 3-second auto-stdin-detect wait. Partition prose explains the discipline: heredoc-on-stdin for prompt-bearing children (STE-185), `< /dev/null` for non-prompt-bearing children (this FR). End state: every Phase 2 spawn has explicit stdin handling. (STE-188)
- **STE-189 — `/setup` scaffold-deliverable inventory + restrictive-prompt rule.** Step 8 now names the six artifact classes `/setup` produces (`CLAUDE.md`, `.claude/settings.json`, `.mcp.json`, `specs/{requirements,technical-spec,testing-spec}.md`, `specs/plan/M1.md` + `.gitkeep` stubs, `src/.placeholder.test.ts` on Bun) with explicit "/setup deliverable, emitted unconditionally" labels. Restrictive driver phrasing ("only /setup completes here", "do not run /spec-write", "minimal mode") constrains downstream skills, not /setup's own deliverables — codified to prevent the LLM-misread that caused Jira-run-2 F2. (STE-189)
- **STE-191 — Pre-flight #8 single-hit name-match KEY surfacing.** When `mcp__atlassian__getVisibleJiraProjects(searchString=<X>)` returns exactly one entry whose `name` matched but `key` did NOT (the unambiguous "operator passed display name instead of KEY" case), the refusal now names the matching Space's KEY and tells the operator exactly which `--jira-project <KEY>` to retry with. Empty / multi-hit responses keep the generic refusal — surfacing one KEY out of zero or N would mislead. The defensive gate stays; only the message sharpens. (STE-191)

Total test count at release: 1447 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.4.0] — 2026-05-01 — "Janitor"

Smoke-findings cleanup milestone (5 FRs from the 2026-05-01 Linear + Jira smoke runs against v2.3.0). Closes the `??` toolkit-files trap on the canonical `/setup → /spec-write → /implement → /gate-check` chain, adds a probe #14 carve-out for the legitimate post-single-FR "milestone ready to close" state, documents the `/implement <FR-id>` vs `M<N>` Phase-5 divergence with a new doc-existence probe, sharpens `/spec-write` filename-policy-override prose for the no-user-override path, and drops the misleading `(v0.1.0)` suffix from `/setup`'s bootstrap commit subject (replaced by a `Toolkit:` body footer).

### Added

- **STE-179 — `/spec-write` commits its `specs/` outputs (Step 7a).** New Step 7a stages every file written under `specs/` and produces one commit per `/spec-write` invocation: `chore(specs): write FR <tracker-id>` for new-FR runs, `docs(specs): edit cross-cutting specs` otherwise. Auto / `-p` mode default-applies `y` and emits a `spec_write_commit_default_applied` row in the Step 7 summary; `n` decline leaves files staged with a `spec_write_commit_declined` advisory. Probe #22 renamed `setup-bootstrap-committed` → `toolkit-bootstrap-committed`; scan-set widened from `CLAUDE.md` only to `CLAUDE.md` + `.claude/settings.json` + `.mcp.json` + every active file under `specs/` (archive excluded). (STE-179)
- **STE-180 — `/gate-check` probe #14 fully-checked-single-FR carve-out.** Widens STE-151's carve-out: when the single-FR `/implement <FR-id>` run completes the milestone's last unchecked task (plan has zero `[ ]` lines, FR file still `status: active`, ticket Done), probe #14 now passes with an advisory `M<N> plan fully checked but not archived — run /spec-archive M<N> or /implement M<N> to close` rather than reporting drift. New `fullyCheckedSingleFrExempt` predicate added to `active_ticket_drift_predicate.ts` alongside the existing `singleFrCleanExempt`. M23-class drift detection (Phase 1 step 0.c skipped, wrong assignee, malformed-plan boundary `total = 0`) preserved unchanged. (STE-180)
- **STE-181 — `/implement` SKILL.md `## Invocation forms` section.** New section after the lede with a side-by-side phase-comparison table showing the `<FR-id>` vs `M<N>` divergence at Phase 5 (`silent-skip` vs `runs it`); names canonical use cases and cross-references STE-180's advisory. `/spec-write` Step 7 closing-summary `Next:` line tightens — new-FR runs recommend the FR-id form, cross-cutting-only runs recommend `M<N>`. Smoke-driver SKILL.md gains a post-Phase-4 advisory clarifying the single-FR end state. New conformance probe `implement-invocation-grammar-doc` (gate-check #31) enforces the documentation shape: heading present + table ≥6 rows + Phase-5 row carries both `silent-skip` and `runs it` literals. Vacuous on projects that don't ship the toolkit's own SKILL.md. (STE-181)
- **STE-183 — `setup-bootstrap-commit-subject` probe (gate-check #30).** Scans the most recent `chore: bootstrap dev-process-toolkit*` commit and asserts the subject is exactly `chore: bootstrap dev-process-toolkit` (no parenthesized version suffix), AND the body either has no `Toolkit:` line or carries exactly one `^Toolkit: dev-process-toolkit v\d+\.\d+\.\d+$` line. Backwards-compat carve-out: commits authored before 2026-05-01T00:00:00Z pass vacuously (covers downstream repos whose bootstrap commit predates this FR). Vacuous on non-git repos and when no matching commit exists. (STE-183)

### Changed

- **STE-182 — `/spec-write` `filename_policy_override` row renders conditionally.** Static plain-language map row collapses two variants: `(a) no user override: FR filename derived from tracker policy (Provider.filenameFor) → <filename> (no user override)` for the common pre-baked-stub path, `(b) user override: ... → <filename> (overrode user-proposed: <user-name>)` when the user typed an explicit alternative filename. The pre-fix prose `the user-proposed name was overridden by the adapter convention` read as a false-positive on every run; the conditional preserves the unconditional-emit rule (row still fires on every tracker-mode FR write/import) and the `mode: none` exemption verbatim. Annotation blockquote below the row documents which variant fires when. (STE-182)
- **STE-183 — `/setup` bootstrap commit subject + `Toolkit:` footer.** Subject changes from `chore: bootstrap dev-process-toolkit (v0.1.0)` to `chore: bootstrap dev-process-toolkit` — the `(v0.1.0)` referenced the project's `bun init` default, not the toolkit version. New `Toolkit: dev-process-toolkit v<plugin-version>` body footer appended after `Refs:` carries the actual toolkit version read from `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/.claude-plugin/plugin.json`. Read is fault-tolerant: missing/corrupt `plugin.json` → footer absent (no malformed `v<unknown>` line) + Step 7 advisory under `setup_toolkit_version_unreadable`. Bootstrap commit's load-bearing role takes priority over the audit footer. (STE-183)

Total test count at release: 1438 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.3.0] — 2026-05-01 — "Socratic"

Single-FR milestone tightening `/setup`'s prompt sequencing to match the one-question-at-a-time discipline `/brainstorm` and `/spec-write` already enforce. Extracts the rule into a canonical `docs/patterns.md § Pattern 26` so future skills inherit by reference.

### Changed

- **STE-177 — `/setup` Socratic prompt sequencing + shared `docs/patterns.md` rule.** Step 7d's lede no longer reads "Three yes/no prompts in this exact order" (LLM read this as "ask the trio in one turn"); rewritten to "Ask one at a time, in this order — wait for each answer before asking the next." New top-level Rules bullet names steps 7b/7c/7d/7e and forbids bundling. New `## Pattern 26: Socratic Prompting {#pattern-socratic-prompting}` in `docs/patterns.md` extracts `/brainstorm`'s rationalization-prevention table as the canonical cross-skill rule; `/setup`, `/spec-write`, and `/brainstorm` reference it by anchor.
