## [2.2.0] — 2026-05-01 — "Polish"

Smoke #6 (Jira) + smoke #7 (Linear) follow-up. Six FRs harden the `/implement` Stage D archive flow, sharpen `/spec-review`'s drift signaling, document conditional behaviors that prior smoke runs flagged as undocumented, and extend the `/smoke-test` driver with scratch reset, by-key team probe, `--reset`, ghost detector, and Jira comment-path coverage.

### Added

- **STE-172 — `/spec-review` live-spec drift refresh hint.** New `formatDriftHint(count)` helper in `adapters/_shared/src/spec_review_drift_hint.ts` owns the canonical line shape; SKILL.md emits `Live-spec refresh suggested — N drift(s) found in cross-cutting specs; consider rerunning /spec-write before next /implement.` after the verdict when `drift_count >= 2`. Threshold (`>= 2` not `> 0`) suppresses single-line cosmetic drifts during normal `/implement` churn so operators don't learn to ignore the hint. (STE-172)
- **STE-176 — `/smoke-test` coverage extension.** Optional Jira-only pre-flight #9 JQLs `project = <KEY> AND labels = "dpt-smoke" AND status != "Done"` and warns when ghost-cluster count exceeds threshold (default 5); Linear path skips. New Phase 2 stand-alone `mcp__atlassian__addCommentToJiraIssue` probe closes AC-STE-154.9 AC 6 coverage gap (chosen over side-effect-of-`/implement` to validate the MCP tool independent of narration policy). Runs-table annotation contract records `comment exercised` on post-STE-176 Jira runs. (STE-176)

### Changed

- **STE-171 — `/implement` Stage D archive hardening.** Three holes in the canonical archive flow closed: `appendTraceabilityRow(repoRoot, frId, acNumbers, implFiles, testFiles)` writes one idempotent row per archived FR to `specs/requirements.md` § 6; `isFRUntrackedInPorcelain` + `git add` before `git mv` preserves rename history under `git log --follow`; `cleanupPlanVerifyLines` gains a filesystem fallback (same regex shape as gate-check probe #28) so missing-path verify lines flip even when the LLM forgets `deletedFiles[]`. (STE-171)
- **STE-173 — `/setup` SKILL.md commit-msg hook prose.** Step 6b now states the install is best-effort under non-interactive runs (model-layer block on `.git/hooks/` writes is expected under `bypassPermissions` and logged in `## /setup audit` rather than failing the run) and names the manual fallback (`cp plugins/dev-process-toolkit/templates/git-hooks/commit-msg.sh .git/hooks/commit-msg && chmod +x .git/hooks/commit-msg`). (STE-173)
- **STE-174 — `/simplify` SKILL.md no-op gate-skip prose.** Verify step now documents the conditional: when no refactors are warranted, the gate re-run is skipped — re-running an unchanged tree against a clean gate is wasted tokens; the operator consults the prior `/implement` or `/gate-check` log for the active gate stamp. (STE-174)
- **STE-175 — `/smoke-test` driver hardening.** Phase 0.5 unconditionally `rm -f /tmp/dpt-smoke-prompt-*.txt /tmp/dpt-smoke-<tracker>-*.log` after operator approval (preserving findings + approval files). Pre-flight #5 probes Linear team by `key` first (`get_team` / `list_teams` filtered on `team.key == "<KEY>"`) with name-prefix `query=` only as fallback. New `--reset` flag wires pre-flight #2's existing-dir refusal into an auto `rm -rf ../dpt-test-project-<tracker>`; surfaced in the Phase 0 contract as `RESET: existing ../dpt-test-project-<tracker> will be deleted before run.`. Default behavior unchanged. (STE-175)

Total test count at release: 1358 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.1.0] — 2026-04-30 — "Portable"

End-user portability for `/ship-milestone`, `/gate-check`, and `/implement`. Three audit-driven FRs that decouple the plugin from its own toolkit-internal layout so it can run cleanly inside any host project.

### Added

- **STE-167 — `/ship-milestone` portability via `## Release Files` block.** The release-bump driver moves from a hard-coded four-file checklist to a YAML block in the host's `CLAUDE.md`. New `release_config` module parses the block and bumps each entry by `kind` — `json` / `toml` / `yaml` / `changelog` / `regex`. Per-stack defaults under `examples/{typescript-node,flutter-dart,python,plugin}/release.yml` seed new projects through `/setup`. The toolkit dogfoods the contract via its own block. (STE-167)

### Changed

- **STE-168 — `/gate-check` probe portability.** Probes #9b (`.claude-plugin/plugin.json` version match) and #10 (toolkit `CLAUDE.md.template` grep) wrap their toolkit-internal paths in existence guards. Absent path emits an `n/a` row with a "probe skipped" reason instead of crashing the gate in end-user projects; toolkit-self-runs continue to gate unchanged. (STE-168)
- **STE-169 — `/implement` chain-failure error message.** The chain-failure remedy line no longer points at `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/.claude-plugin/plugin.json`; it now directs the operator to `claude /plugin list`, a host-layout-agnostic check. (STE-169)

Total test count at release: 1289 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [2.0.0] — 2026-04-30 — "Threshold"

Major-version line bump. **No new FRs ship in this release** — v2.0.0 is a deliberate cut over the cumulative post-M36 era, marking the point at which the plugin-facing API stabilizes under SemVer compatibility going forward.

The 2.x line declares the following surfaces stable:

- **Skill set + slash-command surface** — every command exposed under `/dev-process-toolkit:*` is now under MAJOR-bump compatibility. Renames or removals require 2.x → 3.x.
- **`CLAUDE.md` `## Task Tracking` schema** — the `mode:` / `mcp_server:` / `jira_ac_field:` keys + the `### Linear` / `### Jira` sub-section shape (closed set in `task_tracking_canonical_keys.ts`).
- **FR-frontmatter bimodal-identity contract** — `mode: none` carries `id:`; tracker mode carries the compact `tracker: { <mode>: <tracker-id> }` block. The verbose `{ key, id, url }` form is rejected.
- **Adapter contract** — Linear + Jira adapter signatures (`upsertTicketMetadata`, `pullAcs`, `pushAcToggle`, `transitionStatus`, `mintIdentity`) under their current parameter shapes; the `UpsertMetadataInput.labels?: string[]` widening from M44 (v1.44.0) is now part of the canonical contract.

The cumulative span 2.0.0 acknowledges (without re-listing per FR — entries below carry the per-release detail):

- **M36 (v1.37.0) — Conventional Commits adoption.** First canonical CC commit; `commit-msg` hook hard-blocks non-conforming subjects with no grace period.
- **M43 (v1.43.0) — Jira live-MCP conformance.** Adapter spec aligned with live Atlassian Rovo MCP; seven F1–F7 corrections in one FR (snake_case → camelCase tool names, `transition_status` `statusCategory.key` fallback, `description` sentinel for `jira_ac_field`, `Task` default issue type, manual Space pre-creation prerequisite, no `deleteJiraIssue` available).
- **M44 (v1.44.0) — `/smoke-test --tracker jira` branch.** Tier 5 dogfood driver covers both Linear and Jira modes; Atlassian Rovo MCP entry pre-baked; `dpt-smoke` label end-to-end via `UpsertMetadataInput.labels` widening.
- **M45 (v1.45.0) — Idempotency hardening + smoke polish.** Gateway-Timeout retry path widens the JQL idempotency window with `1s + 2s + 4s` backoff before any fresh create; `tracker_idempotency_uncertain` warning row when ambiguous.
- **M46 (v1.46.0) — Per-tracker artifact isolation + No-claim-on-create.** Concurrent two-terminal smoke runs (one Linear, one Jira) without filesystem collision; `/spec-write` invariant: freshly-created tracker tickets land in default state, claim deferred to `/implement` Phase 1.
- **M47 (v1.47.0) — Skill-prose hygiene.** ~280 toolkit-internal `STE-<N>` / `AC-STE-<N>.<M>` cross-references scrubbed from `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/{skills,docs,adapters}/*.md`; provenance moved to FR files + commit history.

### Breaking changes

None at the source level. The 2.x line is the **first SemVer-compatible commitment** for the plugin-facing surface — pre-2.0 the plugin had no users (per project convention; see `project_no_users_yet.md`), and back-compat shims were considered dead weight. Going forward, the surfaces named above are under MAJOR-bump compatibility.

### Migration notes

Pre-2.0 installs do not exist (no marketplace consumers). For internal repos that vendored plugin contents directly: no behavior change in this bump — files are byte-identical to v1.47.0 except for the version string in `plugin.json` and `marketplace.json`. No CLAUDE.md edits required, no FR migration required, no test changes.

Test count at release: 437 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors (unchanged from v1.47.0).

## [1.47.0] — 2026-04-30 — "Plain"

M47 ships a single prose-only FR: a project-wide scrub of toolkit-internal tracker-ID cross-references from active skill prose, operator-facing docs, and adapter operator-facing sections. **STE-161 (low)** removes ~280 inline `STE-<N>` and `AC-STE-<N>.<M>` references across `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/*/SKILL.md` (~189), `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/docs/*.md` (~141), and the operator-facing prose in `adapters/{linear,jira}.md` (~4) — replacing each with plain-language rule names (e.g., `STE-117 workspace binding` → `workspace-binding rule`, `AC-STE-110.4 flip` → "the prior warn-only severity flipped to error"). The downstream-operator argument dominates the rewrite: this plugin is installed in projects that bind to their own tracker (or none), so a Linear-workspace-internal `STE-117` is meaningless jargon to anyone outside our org; provenance for each rule lives in the FR file + commit history, not inline in the skill the LLM reads at runtime. Placeholder forms (`<tracker-id>`, `STE-<N>`, `AC-<tracker-id>.<N>`) are preserved as template markers; adapter-internal helper code (`adapters/_shared/src/*.ts` test names, internal capability keys) is untouched. Verified by `grep -rE 'STE-[0-9]+|AC-STE-[0-9]+' plugins/dev-process-toolkit/{skills/*/SKILL.md,docs/*.md,templates/spec-templates/*.template,adapters/*.md}` returning zero matches across the in-scope tree (excluding placeholder markers). The convention is now one-way: future skill-prose edits in any milestone should not reintroduce inline tracker-ID refs; a `/gate-check` probe enforcing this rule is a possible follow-up FR. Operator-deferred AC-STE-161.6 — post-scrub `/smoke-test` ships `[~]`; M48 carries the retroactive validation. Minor bump — skill-prose changes only; no plugin-facing API change. Test count: 437 → 437 (+0; the 8 skip remain skip).

- **STE-161 — Skill-prose hygiene: scrub toolkit-meta tracker-ID refs.** Removes every `STE-<N>` / `AC-STE-<N>.<M>` cross-reference from `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/*/SKILL.md` (~189 refs across 12 skills), `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/docs/*.md` (~141 across 17 reference docs), and the operator-facing prose in `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/adapters/{linear,jira}.md` (~4 refs in rule-statement subsections). Each ref is either dropped (parenthetical attribution) or rewritten to plain language naming the rule by description. ## [1.46.0] — 2026-04-30 — "Tandem"

M46 ships per-tracker artifact isolation in the project-local `/smoke-test` driver and a "No claim on create" invariant in `/spec-write`. Two FRs in Phase A, both prose-only — no plugin-facing API change. **STE-159 (low)** rewrites every per-run `/smoke-test` artifact to a `<tracker>`-keyed path so two terminals — one Linear, one Jira — can run concurrently in tandem without filesystem collision: test-project basename becomes `../dpt-test-project-{linear,jira}`, every `/tmp/dpt-smoke-*` artifact carries a tracker suffix (findings, per-skill logs, MCP config, approval record). Pre-flight #6's basename check is now a closed two-element allow-list (`{dpt-test-project-linear, dpt-test-project-jira}`); the reference-implementation snippet uses a `case` membership statement so the bare basename, garbage suffixes, and case-mismatched forms all refuse with NFR-10 canonical shape — three new negative cases (`dpt-test-project`, `dpt-test-project-foo`, `dpt-test-project-LINEAR`) join the existing six-case adversarial probe (verified original 2026-04-27 + M46 expansion). A new "Operator-driven parallelism" subsection codifies the two-terminal tandem run: no combined-mode flag, no parent-side fan-out, no merged findings, expected wall-clock win below 2× (~70% of theoretical, ~11–14 min vs. ~10 min solo) because both children bill the same Anthropic key concurrently. The threat-model section is rewritten to the two-basename framing — "scoped to two well-known throwaway directories, one per tracker" — and pre-flight #6 enforces basename membership. **STE-160 (low)** inserts the "No claim on create" invariant in `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/spec-write/SKILL.md` § 0b step 4, immediately before the workspace-binding paragraph: freshly-created tracker tickets MUST land in the tracker's default state (Linear: `Backlog` unassigned; Jira: project start state); `/spec-write` writes the spec, it does not start the work — the claim (Backlog → In Progress + assign me) is `/implement` Phase 1's job. The invariant names both Linear (`save_issue.state` / `assignee`) and Jira (`transitionJiraIssue`) failure modes by canonical MCP-tool name. Origin: an LLM operator running `/spec-write` for STE-159 itself extrapolated from the implement-side claim rule and pre-transitioned the ticket to `In Progress` — caught and reverted manually; this FR documents the fix at the plugin level so the regression cannot recur on the next tracker-mode `/spec-write`. Operator-deferred AC-STE-159.6 (tandem-run smoke) and AC-STE-160.3 (default-state inspection smoke) ship `[~]` — pending an M47 amendment to carry retroactive-validation framing for these two ACs (M47 will roll the smoke gate forward into smoke #8). Minor bump — skill-prose changes only. Test count: 1240 → 1240 (+0).

### Added

- **STE-159 — `/smoke-test` per-tracker artifact isolation + operator-driven parallelism subsection.** `.claude/skills/smoke-test/SKILL.md` rewrites every per-run artifact to a `<tracker>`-keyed path so two terminals (one Linear, one Jira) can run concurrently without filesystem collision. Test-project basename: `../dpt-test-project-{linear,jira}`. `/tmp/dpt-smoke-*` artifacts: findings = `/tmp/dpt-smoke-findings-<date>-<tracker>.md`, per-skill logs = `/tmp/dpt-smoke-<tracker>-<skill>.log`, MCP config = `/tmp/dpt-smoke-mcp-config-<tracker>.json`, approval record = `/tmp/dpt-smoke-<date>-<tracker>-approval.txt`. Pre-flight #2 keys on the per-tracker basename (a Linear run does not refuse just because a concurrent Jira run owns the Jira basename). Pre-flight #6's basename check is now a closed two-element allow-list `{dpt-test-project-linear, dpt-test-project-jira}` enforced via `case` membership; reference-impl snippet updated; the verification comment cites the M46 expansion (canonical-good split into two valid forms; three new negative cases — bare basename, garbage suffix, case-mismatch — added on top of the existing six-case adversarial probe). New "Operator-driven parallelism" subsection (after "When to use") names the supported tandem mode, the rate-limit caveat (~70% of theoretical 2× wall-clock win, ~11–14 min total for tandem vs. ~10 min solo, single Anthropic key), the no-merged-findings invariant (no combined-mode flag, no parent-side fan-out — each terminal owns its own findings, log, and teardown checklist), and the failure-isolation guarantee (a hang in one terminal does not stall the other). Phase 0 contract block, Phase 1 setup print line, Phase 2 child invocation flags (`cwd`, `--mcp-config`, log file), Phase 3 findings template, Phase 4 verify-on-disk paths, Phase 5 Linear + Jira teardown checklists, and the Output section all reflect the renamed paths. Operator-deferred AC-STE-159.6 — tandem clean-run smoke shipped `[~]`; rolls forward into M47's smoke #8. (STE-159)
- **STE-160 — `/spec-write` "No claim on create" invariant.** `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/spec-write/SKILL.md` § 0b step 4 inserts an explicit "No claim on create" invariant paragraph immediately before the workspace-binding paragraph: freshly-created tracker tickets MUST land in the tracker's default state (Linear: `Backlog` unassigned; Jira: the project's start state); do NOT pass `state` / `assignee` (Linear `save_issue`) or pre-transition (Jira `transitionJiraIssue`) on the create call. The invariant prose names both adapters' canonical MCP-tool semantics by name so the rule is unambiguous regardless of which adapter the operator's project binds to. Cites the rationale (a ticket sitting in `In Progress` before any code work begins misrepresents board state and trips downstream `/gate-check` active-side drift probes that expect `In Progress` to mean active development) and the claim-handoff site (`/implement` Phase 1, not `/spec-write`). Origin: an LLM operator running `/spec-write` for STE-159 itself extrapolated from the implement-side claim rule and pre-transitioned the freshly-created Linear ticket to `In Progress` + assigned; the user caught the regression on the spot, reverted manually, and asked for a plugin-level fix instead of a memory-only fix. Plugin > memory for facts that travel to all downstream operators. Operator-deferred AC-STE-160.3 — `/smoke-test` confirms the contract end-to-end; rolls forward into M47's smoke #8 alongside AC-STE-159.6. (STE-160)

## [1.45.0] — 2026-04-30 — "Backoff"

M45 closes the smoke #6 + #7 follow-up FRs that the M44 risk table routed via the `M44-followup` Linear label. Two FRs ship in one bundled atomic commit. **STE-157 (medium)** hardens `/spec-write`'s tracker-mode `upsertTicketMetadata(null, ...)` retry path against the orphan-duplicate failure mode that smoke #6 finding F6 surfaced (the create call returned a Gateway-Timeout while the server-side write had landed; the single-shot JQL idempotency probe missed the eventual-consistency window; the retry created an orphan-stub second ticket). The retry path now widens the idempotency window with three backoff probes — `1s + 2s + 4s` — before any fresh create fires; persistent miss after backoff surfaces a `tracker_idempotency_uncertain` warning row in /spec-write Step 7 so the operator manually verifies before downstream skills bind to the new id. `adapters/jira.md` § `upsert_ticket_metadata` documents the full schedule + fallback table; `adapters/linear.md` carries the symmetric one-line note (Linear's `save_issue` has the same Gateway-Timeout class of failure mode, even though smoke #6 surfaced the defect on Jira only). **STE-158 (low / bundle)** rolls up four smoke-side cosmetic / operator-UX polish items: (F1 Linear) /spec-write Step 7 prose explicitly fires in `claude -p` non-interactive runs even when no questions were asked (smoke #7 1-byte-stdout regression); (F1 Jira) /implement Phase 4 + /spec-archive single-FR + `docs/implement-reference.md` § Milestone Archival spec full ISO-8601 `archived_at` (date+time+Z, never date-only `T00:00:00Z` — pedantic prose so the LLM-rendered timestamp can't drift back to midnight UTC); (F2 Jira) /gate-check post-archive conformance-probes summary line uses canonical `[N active, M vacuous]` shape — operator-parseable, distinguishes active probes from FR-traversal probes that early-returned because no active FRs remained post-archive; (F5 Jira) /spec-write tracker mode unconditionally surfaces a `filename_policy_override` row regardless of whether the user proposed an alternative filename (mode: none is exempt — short-ULID is local-mint, never policy-overridden). Four new doc-conformance probe files (`spec-write-jira-retry-idempotency.test.ts`, `implement-archived-at-precision.test.ts`, `gate-check-post-archive-counts.test.ts`, `spec-write-step7-tracker-id-rendering.test.ts`) plus AC-STE-158.1 lock added to the existing `spec-write-final-summary.test.ts`. Shared `specWriteStep7Map` helper hoisted to `tests/_skill-md.ts` so the two consumers don't drift. Operator-deferred AC-STE-157.5 / AC-STE-158.5 — `/smoke-test --tracker jira --jira-project DST` smoke #8 re-runs against the post-fix tree before /ship-milestone M45 closes; same operator-deferred-smoke pattern as M44. Minor bump — skill-prose changes + new test fixtures; no plugin-facing API change. Test count: 1217 → 1240 (+23).

### Added

- **STE-157 — /spec-write idempotency hardening on Gateway-Timeout retry.** `skills/spec-write/SKILL.md` § 0b step 4 adds the canonical backoff retry contract for tracker-mode `upsertTicketMetadata(null, ...)`: on a network-error response (Gateway-Timeout / 504 / connection reset / equivalent), the retry path runs the JQL idempotency probe with three backoff attempts (`1s + 2s + 4s`) before falling through to a fresh create. The existing single-shot probe stays as the fast path (no extra latency on the success path). If any backoff attempt finds the original write, no duplicate create is issued. If all three backoff probes still miss, fall through to a fresh create AND surface a `tracker_idempotency_uncertain` warning row in /spec-write Step 7. New static map row added to the Step 7 plain-language table: `tracker_idempotency_uncertain` ⇒ `idempotency probe still ambiguous after backoff retry — possible duplicate ticket; operator should manually verify before downstream skills bind to the new id`. `adapters/jira.md` § `upsert_ticket_metadata` carries the full retry-with-backoff schedule table (one row per attempt with the wait time and JQL search action) + the still-ambiguous fallback (warning row) + the out-of-scope note (Atlassian Rovo MCP does not currently expose idempotency-key headers; revisit if a future MCP version surfaces them). `adapters/linear.md` § `upsert_ticket_metadata` carries the one-line symmetric note that Linear's `save_issue` shares the same Gateway-Timeout class of failure mode. New test file `tests/spec-write-jira-retry-idempotency.test.ts` (10 doc-conformance asserts) locks the prose contracts: spec-write step 4 names the schedule + JQL probe + Gateway-Timeout trigger + single-shot fast path + still-ambiguous fallback; Step 7 plain-language map carries the canonical key + operator-actionable rendered prose; jira.md upsert section names schedule + 3-attempt count + fallback key; linear.md upsert section names Gateway-Timeout failure mode + backoff. Operator-deferred AC-STE-157.5 — smoke #8 re-run against the post-fix tree gates /ship-milestone (run window check: only the FR's own canonical issue plus pre-existing orphans in the run window). Closes smoke #6 finding F6. (STE-157)

### Changed

- **STE-158 — Smoke #6+#7 minor polish bundle (-p stdout, archived_at precision, gate-check probe-count, filename-override).** Four prose-only fixes bundled into one FR per the M44 risk-table policy. **F1 (Linear) — /spec-write Step 7 fires in claude -p runs.** `skills/spec-write/SKILL.md` Step 7 adds the "Non-interactive / `-p` mode firing rule" paragraph explicitly mandating that the closing summary block emit even when no questions were asked (the smoke #7 regression: -p mode produced 1-byte stdout because the LLM short-circuited Step 7 on the silent path). The existing `>=100 byte` floor is the regression signal that the summary fired at all. **F1 (Jira) — full ISO-8601 archived_at across the archival path.** `skills/implement/SKILL.md` § Milestone Archival, `skills/spec-archive/SKILL.md` single-FR archive, and `docs/implement-reference.md` § Phase 4 Milestone Archival each spec the canonical timestamp shape pedantically: full ISO-8601 with date + time + Z (e.g., `2026-04-30T17:23:11Z`), never date-only with zeroed time (`2026-04-30T00:00:00Z` is the regression shape). The render-via call is now explicit: `date -u +%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ`, never the shorter `date +%Y-%m-%d` form (which rounds to midnight UTC — the smoke #6 finding F1 root cause). **F2 (Jira) — /gate-check post-archive summary line.** `skills/gate-check/SKILL.md` § Conformance-probes summary line defines the canonical roll-up shape `conformance-probes pass: <N>/<N> [<active> active, <vacuous> vacuous]` and explains what counts as a vacuous probe post-archive (FR-traversal probes that early-return when no active FRs remain — probes #1 / #2 / #7 / #8 / #14 / #15 / #25 / #26 / #27). The bracketed shape is operator-parseable; the previous `(most vacuous post-archive)` parenthetical was soft. **F5 (Jira) — /spec-write filename_policy_override row.** `skills/spec-write/SKILL.md` Step 7 plain-language map gains a new key: `filename_policy_override` ⇒ `FR filename derived from tracker policy (Provider.filenameFor) — the user-proposed name was overridden by the adapter convention`. Tracker-mode runs surface the row unconditionally on every successful FR write or import, regardless of whether the user proposed an alternative filename. `mode: none` is exempt — short-ULID stems are local-mint via `Provider.mintId()`, never policy-overridden. Three new test files (`tests/implement-archived-at-precision.test.ts`, `tests/gate-check-post-archive-counts.test.ts`, `tests/spec-write-step7-tracker-id-rendering.test.ts`) cover the three codifiable F1/Jira / F2 / F5 fixes; AC-STE-158.1 (-p firing rule) is locked by extension to `tests/spec-write-final-summary.test.ts`. Shared `specWriteStep7Map(body)` helper extracted to `tests/_skill-md.ts` so the two consumers (`spec-write-jira-retry-idempotency.test.ts` + `spec-write-step7-tracker-id-rendering.test.ts`) don't drift. Operator-deferred AC-STE-158.5 — same smoke #8 gate as STE-157.5. Closes smoke #6 findings F1 / F2 / F5 + smoke #7 finding F1. (STE-158)

Total test count at release: 1240 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [1.43.0] — 2026-04-29 — "Sentinel"

M43 lands one /smoke-test run #5 fix. STE-154 aligns `adapters/jira.md` with the live Atlassian Rovo MCP after the first Tier 5 manual conformance pass against `stellartechlab.atlassian.net` (the prerequisite that v1.0–v1.42 lacked — the provisional adapter spec was authored from public Rovo docs alone). Closes Phase H Task 2 by collapsing seven smoke-#5 discrepancies (F1–F7) into a single doc-and-config FR. Most-severe finding (F7): the spec MCP tool names were snake_case (`get_issue`, `update_issue`, `transition_issue`, `get_transitions`, `create_issue`); live names are camelCase + `Jira` infix (`getJiraIssue`, `editJiraIssue`, `transitionJiraIssue`, `getTransitionsForJiraIssue`, `createJiraIssue`, `addCommentToJiraIssue`) — the adapter as written could not dispatch a single call. F1 adds a `to.statusCategory.key` fallback to `transition_status` so default Kanban templates (To Do / In Progress / Done) work zero-config; `in_review` collapses to `indeterminate`. F2 documents the `contentFormat: "markdown"` parameter on `pull_acs` / `push_ac_toggle` / `upsert_ticket_metadata` / `addCommentToJiraIssue`. F3 extends the existing top-level Schema L key `jira_ac_field:` to accept the sentinel value `description` alongside `customfield_XXXXX` — when discovery returns `{ ok: false }` (the canonical state for team-managed Kanban templates that ship without an AC custom field), `/setup` prompts the operator to either create a custom field and re-run, or persist `jira_ac_field: description` so AC reads/writes target the issue description body's `## Acceptance Criteria` section. No new canonical key (`task_tracking_canonical_keys.ts` closed set unmodified). F4 swaps the hard-coded `issuetype="Story"` in `upsert_ticket_metadata` for a `Task` default + `jira_issue_type:` override in the `### Jira` block — Kanban projects ship Task/Epic/Subtask only. F5 documents the manual Space pre-creation prerequisite + `getVisibleJiraProjects` visibility probe (refuses with NFR-10 canonical shape on miss). F6 documents that `deleteJiraIssue` is not exposed by the MCP — `/spec-archive` for Jira transitions to Done, never deletes. All "Status: provisional (Phase H conformance)" warning blocks removed and replaced with one-line "Verified against live MCP 2026-04-29 (smoke-test #5)" provenance (F8/AC-STE-154.8). Smoke #5 trace at `specs/notes/jira-smoke-5.md` captures step 1 (`getVisibleJiraProjects`) live-verified; steps 2–6 partial (live writes deferred to a later operator-driven smoke run). Minor bump — extends `jira_ac_field:` value semantics with the `description` sentinel and adds operator-visible /setup prose for the Jira branch. Test count: 1196 → 1215 (+19).

### Fixed

- **STE-154 — `adapters/jira.md` Phase H live-MCP conformance.** Aligns the Jira adapter spec with the live Atlassian Rovo MCP after smoke-test run #5 against `stellartechlab.atlassian.net`. Seven F1–F7 corrections in one FR: (F1) `transition_status` falls back to `to.statusCategory.key` when no exact `to.name` match exists, with `canonicalCategory(in_review) = indeterminate` collapsing the two when the workflow has no exact `In Review` named state — default Kanban templates work zero-config; (F2) `contentFormat: "markdown"` documented on the four write/read ops so markdown round-trips without ADF conversion; (F3) extends top-level Schema L key `jira_ac_field:` to accept the sentinel value `description` alongside `customfield_XXXXX` — `/setup` prompts on `discover_field.ts` `{ ok: false }` (which fires on team-managed Kanban templates that ship no AC custom field) and persists either choice; no new canonical key, no implicit fallback; (F4) `upsert_ticket_metadata` defaults `issueTypeName: "Task"` with `jira_issue_type:` in `### Jira` overriding — Kanban projects don't have `Story`; (F5) `/setup` for `mode: jira` documents manual Space pre-creation and validates `project_key` visibility via `getVisibleJiraProjects`, refusing with NFR-10 canonical shape on miss; (F6) `deleteJiraIssue` documented as unavailable on the MCP — `/spec-archive` transitions to Done, never deletes; (F7) MCP tool table uses live camelCase names (`getJiraIssue`, `editJiraIssue`, `transitionJiraIssue`, `getTransitionsForJiraIssue`, `createJiraIssue`, `addCommentToJiraIssue`) — adapter can now actually dispatch. ## [1.42.0] — 2026-04-29 — "Provenance"

M42 lands one /smoke-test run #4 fix. STE-153 closes the all-explicit-answer gap in `/setup`'s `## /setup audit` synthesis: when the harness pre-baked all five Schema L answers (the canonical autonomous-mode path), step 7b/7c/7d's per-step `appendAuditEntry` calls were skipped (they only fired on default-applied outcomes), and step 8a's `synthesizeAuditSection` either no-oped on an empty resolved-defaults table or threw `AuditPostconditionUnsatisfiable`. The resulting `CLAUDE.md` landed without `## /setup audit`, and `/gate-check` probe #19 (`setup-audit-section-presence`) hard-failed on the next pass — toolkit marker present, `branch_template:` populated, `## Docs` present, audit heading absent. The fix flips the recording contract: every Schema L resolution at 7b/7c/7d records into the resolved-values table with a per-entry `reason:` field (`"user-supplied"` or `"default applied"`), so step 8a's synthesizer always has the full set of candidates to materialize. Renames `ResolvedDefaults` → `ResolvedSchemaLValues` and `ResolvedDefaultEntry<T>` → `ResolvedSchemaLEntry<T>` (no users yet — alias dropped). Probe #19 stays as-is (single source of truth for the trigger predicate); `AuditPostconditionUnsatisfiable` becomes truly unreachable on a well-formed run, with updated JSDoc clarifying it remains as a defensive invariant. Minor bump — extends the audit log with new `reason: "user-supplied"` entries that previously left no trace; existing default-applied bullets still land byte-identically. Test count: 1187 → 1196 (+9).

### Fixed

- **STE-153 — /setup synthesizes `## /setup audit` on every Schema L resolution.** Closes the canonical autonomous-mode path break where `/setup` ran with all five Schema L answers pre-baked (the most common scripted/CI scenario): the resulting `CLAUDE.md` landed without the `## /setup audit` section and `/gate-check` probe #19 hard-failed on the next pass. Recording contract now flows on `/setup`'s side — every resolved value at steps 7b/7c/7d (user-supplied or default-applied) records into the in-scope resolved Schema L values table with a per-entry `reason:` field. Step 8a's `synthesizeAuditSection` runs unconditionally when at least one Schema L surface is populated (`branch_template:` populated **or** `## Docs` present) and produces the audit section as a deterministic byproduct of every well-formed `/setup` run, not only of default-applied outcomes. Idempotent re-run with conflicting `reason` for the same `(step, field)` is a skip, not an overwrite, preserving STE-108's append-only contract. Renames internal types `ResolvedDefaults` → `ResolvedSchemaLValues` and `ResolvedDefaultEntry<T>` → `ResolvedSchemaLEntry<T>` (alias dropped — no users yet). Probe #19 trigger predicate `hasDefaultApplicableOutcomes` keeps its current shape; only the prose around it is reframed (FR Technical Design's "no probe code change" rule). New end-to-end fixture `tests/setup-audit-all-explicit.test.ts` locks the all-explicit, all-default, mixed, and `mode: none` + 7c-skip scenarios via `synthesize → probe`. Closes /smoke-test run #4 finding F1. (STE-153)

Total test count at release: 1196 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [1.41.0] — 2026-04-29 — "Exempt"

M41 lands one /smoke-test run #4 fix. STE-151 relaxes /gate-check probe #14 ("Ticket-state drift — active side") to exempt the single-FR-clean state — Done ticket + active FR + plan with unchecked tasks now passes, recognising the canonical mid-milestone shape that `/implement <FR-id>` Phase 4 Close produces. M23 drift cases (Backlog ticket, wrong assignee) and the "forgot bulk archive before /ship-milestone" regression (Done + all-checked + still-active plan) keep firing. Pure prose + predicate edit; no migration, no schema change, no tracker-side behaviour change. Minor bump — adds a new exemption surface visible to /gate-check operators. Test count: 1145 → 1187 (+42).

### Fixed

- **STE-151 — /gate-check probe #14 exempts single-FR-clean state.** Previously, `/gate-check` probe #14 fired a spurious **GATE FAILED** after `/implement <FR-id>` landed a single FR cleanly: Phase 4 Close transitioned the Linear ticket to **Done**, but `specs/frs/<FR-id>.md` intentionally stayed `status: active` per the milestone-bulk-archive design (`skills/implement/SKILL.md` § Milestone Archival). Probe #14's strict assertion (`status == in_progress AND assignee == currentUser`) then failed against the just-released ticket. The relaxation adds a single-FR-clean exemption: when the ticket is in `status_mapping.done` AND the FR's milestone plan is `status: active` AND has at least one unchecked task line, the probe skips the strict assertion. The exemption strictly weakens the predicate — every prior failing case still fails, and the failure-row shape (ULID + tracker ID + observed/expected status + observed/expected assignee) is unchanged for AC-STE-87.4(d) compatibility. Two new pure-function helpers: `readPlanTaskState(specsDir, milestone)` reads the plan task-list state; `activeTicketDriftPasses(summary, planTaskState, statusMapping, currentUser)` composes `inProgressMatches(...) || singleFrCleanExempt(...)`. Closes /smoke-test run #4 finding F-S4-1. (STE-151)

Total test count at release: 1187 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [1.38.0] — 2026-04-28 — "Tighten"

M38 ships **branch ship-readiness** — four audit findings cleared before the long-running `feat/m12-tracker-integration` branch can merge to `main`. The 24-release stretch (v1.15.0 → v1.37.1) shipped 153 archived FRs and a structurally healthy toolkit; the 2026-04-27 audit (8 rounds, 35 findings, 5 zero-finding rounds) converged on a small mandatory set: a silent data-loss path in the resolver, a missing dogfood-side `## Docs` section, internal-namespace leaks in shipped templates, and a self-drifted Release Checklist. Four FRs, all small, independently bisectable. Minor bump: STE-137 alters user-visible template output.

### Fixed

- **STE-135 — `findFRByTrackerRef` no longer silently overwrites local edits in tracker mode.** STE-76 (M21) removed the `id:` line from tracker-mode FR frontmatter, but the resolver still required it — tracker-mode lookups always returned null, falling through to `importFromTracker`'s unconditional `writeFileSync` and clobbering local edits. Fix uses the FR's recommended Path B: a new `findFRPathByTrackerRef(specsDir, key, id, options)` helper in `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/adapters/_shared/src/resolve.ts` returns the file path on hit (no `id:` requirement), and skill prose in `/spec-write` § 0a, `/spec-archive` § 0a, and `/implement` § 0.b′ branches on mode at the resolver-entry step — tracker mode uses the new helper, `mode: none` keeps the original `findFRByTrackerRef` (now mode-none-only with a JSDoc note pointing at the new helper). Test coverage: `tests/resolver-single-pattern.test.ts` rewritten against post-STE-76 fixtures (no `id:` line, populated `tracker.<key>`) — the new row exercises AC-STE-135.7's "hit not null" contract. `docs/resolver-entry.md` decision table updated to reflect the mode-aware split. Reproduced live during the audit against `specs/frs/archive/STE-134.md`. (STE-135)
- **STE-136 — repo's own `CLAUDE.md` carries `## Docs` so probe #18 is green; repo-self-check added.** The dogfood `CLAUDE.md` predates STE-107 (M29) — `## Docs` was never appended, so probe #18 (`claudemd-docs-section-present`, error severity post-M29 STE-110) fired one violation against the live repo. `bun test` reported green only because `tests/gate-check-claudemd-docs-section.test.ts` exercised synthetic temp-dir fixtures with no repo-self-check. Fix: append `## Docs` with the dogfood-correct flags (`user_facing_mode: false`, `packages_mode: false`, `changelog_ci_owned: false` — the plugin's docs ARE the artifact, single package, hand-maintained CHANGELOG). Repo-self-check row added to the probe test (`AC-STE-136.3 — claudemd-docs-section-present runs clean on this repo's baseline`) mirroring `tests/gate-check-root-hygiene.test.ts:262-308`. Doubles as the canonical "F0 illustrates F3a" exhibit — the broader probe-self-check backfill across 23 probes lands as M39 STE-139. (STE-136)
- **STE-138 — `## Release Checklist` in `CLAUDE.md` matches reality.** Two drift bugs in the same paragraph: (G20) the prose claimed "**these four files** MUST all be updated together" but `specs/requirements.md:7` carries the `**Latest shipped release:**` line that has to flip every release — actual count is **five**, current sync was enforced by manual discipline; (G21) the README pointer named `## Structure`, but README's actual section is `## What's Inside` — a release-day reader doing `Cmd-F` for "## Structure" finds nothing and silently misses the count refresh. Fix: bump prose to "five files," add a new bullet for `specs/requirements.md`, and replace `## Structure` → `## What's Inside`. New regression test `tests/release-checklist-consistency.test.ts` enumerates the numbered list, asserts each path exists, every backticked `## <heading>` (excluding "add a new" additive entries) resolves in the target file, and the prose file-count claim matches the list length. Without the test, the same drift recurs on every checklist edit. (STE-138)

### Changed

- **STE-137 — internal `STE-N` / `M<N>` namespace stripped from shipped templates + examples (Tier-1).** `templates/CLAUDE.md.template`, `templates/spec-templates/{requirements,plan,testing-spec}.md.template`, `templates/docs-architecture.md.template`, and `examples/bun-typescript.md` no longer leak this repo's internal ticket / milestone IDs into surfaces that copy into adopting projects. Adapter docs, skill prose, and the `~700-ref` `docs/` sweep are explicitly OUT of scope here — Tier-2 and Tier-3 cleanup land in M39 STE-143. (STE-137)

## [1.37.1] — 2026-04-27 — "Disambiguate"

M37 ships a single user-facing FR: a one-paragraph prose tightening in `skills/spec-write/SKILL.md` § 0b step 1 that scopes ULID minting to `mode: none` and tells the tracker-mode reader to skip step 1. The "always local" qualifier on `Provider.mintId()` described *where* minting happens, not *whether* to mint — a tracker-mode operator walking § 0b top-to-bottom could land on step 1 and propose the call, only to be caught downstream by TypeScript (STE-85: `TrackerProvider` does not implement `IdentityMinter`) or `buildFRFrontmatter` (STE-76 forbids `id:` alongside `trackerBinding`). The runtime guarantees were already firm; the prose just leaked the wrong instruction to a reader following the steps in order. Single-FR milestone, patch bump (no public surface change). Test count: 1071 → 1071 (no test changes — the bug class is "ambiguous prose," caught by review, not assertion). Triggered by a parallel session walking into the structural violation; the fix is one paragraph, the discovery cost was a session-recovery turn.

### Fixed

- **STE-134 — `/spec-write` § 0b step 1 prose scoped to `mode: none`.** `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/spec-write/SKILL.md:47` rewritten via Option A (bifurcate step 1) from the FR's Technical Design: step 1 now leads with `**\`mode: none\` only:**` and continues "**Tracker mode skips this step**: `TrackerProvider` does not implement `IdentityMinter` (STE-85 capability boundary — `mintId()` on a `Provider`-typed value is a TypeScript error by design), and `buildFRFrontmatter(spec, trackerBinding)` rejects `id:` alongside `trackerBinding` (STE-76 / AC-STE-110.2). The tracker ID returned by step 4 is the canonical identity in tracker mode." Walking § 0b top-to-bottom in tracker mode now never lands on a step that prescribes `Provider.mintId()`. Verification: `grep -nE "Provider\.mintId" plugins/dev-process-toolkit/skills/spec-write/SKILL.md` returns exactly one hit (line 47, inside the mode-none-scoped sentence); `/gate-check` clean (probes #11/#13/#14/#15/#23/#25/#26/#27/#28 all green). No code change, no template change, no new test. Out of scope (future FRs): the same prose-clarity audit for the other tracker-mode-conditional steps in § 0b; an automated probe asserting every numbered step in § 0b carries an explicit mode-scope when the underlying behavior is mode-conditional. (STE-134)

Total test count at release: 1071 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

## [1.37.0] — 2026-04-27 — "Conventional"

M36 ships a single user-facing FR: the cutover from the bespoke `M<N>: vX.Y.Z "Codename" — title (STE-<N>)` commit-message form used for M1–M35 to [Conventional Commits v1.0.0](https://www.conventionalcommits.org/en/v1.0.0/), enforced by a local `commit-msg` hook installed by `/setup`. Hybrid posture: pure POSIX-shell hook by default (zero-dep, works on Flutter / Python / mode-none projects); opt-in commitlint variant via `/setup --commitlint` for projects with Node/Bun tooling. Dogfooded — this repo's M36 implementation commit and this very ship commit are the first two canonical CC commits on `main`, both validated by the same hook before they could land. M1–M35 commit history is intentionally pre-CC and not rewritten. Single-FR milestone, minor bump (new public surface: hook template + `--commitlint` flag + `## Commit Convention` section in the CLAUDE.md template). Test count: 1049 → 1071 (+22 — fixture-driven shell-hook test plus updated assertion in the existing `ship-milestone-shape.test.ts` for the new CC release-commit form).

### Added

- **STE-133 — Conventional Commits v1.0.0 enforcement: commit-msg hook template + skill prose + `/setup` integration.** New `plugins/dev-process-toolkit/templates/git-hooks/commit-msg.sh` (~40 lines POSIX shell) validates the message file passed as `$1`: subject regex `^(feat|fix|docs|style|refactor|perf|test|build|ci|chore|revert)(\([^)]+\))?!?: .+` plus ≤72-char length check; empty / comment-only messages allowed (interactive abort path); on invalid, exits 1 with stderr naming the failing rule (`type-prefix-missing` / `unknown-type` / `missing-colon-or-description` / `subject-too-long`) and the offending subject verbatim. Companion `commit-msg.commitlint.sh` delegates to `bunx commitlint --edit "$1"` for projects opting into full spec coverage; `commitlint.config.js` extends `@commitlint/config-conventional`. `/setup` step 6b installs the hook (default + `--commitlint` branches with idempotency tier — missing/byte-identical/different+diff prompt+manual install command on decline); `/setup` does NOT run `bun install` or `bun add` — the install command is surfaced for the user. `/implement` Phase 4 step 15 commit-message section instructs CC subject `<type>(<scope>): <title>` with a type heuristic (`feat` default, `fix`/`docs`/`chore`/`refactor` per FR class) + scope rule + `Refs: STE-<N>` footer, with the proposed type/scope rendered at the step 14 approval gate before commit; full type table + canonical example in `docs/implement-reference.md` § Commit message format (STE-133). `/ship-milestone` release-commit emits `chore(release): vX.Y.Z` with `Release: vX.Y.Z "<Codename>"` and `Refs: M<N>` footers; `/pr` PR title mirrors the feature commit's CC subject ≤72 chars. `templates/CLAUDE.md.template` and root `CLAUDE.md` gain `## Commit Convention` sections (CC v1.0.0 required, `Refs:` footer, `!` for breaking, three sample messages + commitlint opt-in note). Root `CLAUDE.md` notes M36-forward CC enforcement and that M1–M35 history is intentionally not rewritten — the user-prefs `## Git Commit Messages` style override (no Claude attribution, no robot emoji, short and humorous) composes with CC's format constraint. README `## Workflow` paragraph picks up a one-sentence CC-enforcement mention. Test coverage: `tests/conventional-commits-hook.test.ts` exercises the shell hook via `Bun.spawn` against 24 fixtures (6 valid: vanilla `feat:`, scoped `fix(adapters/linear):`, breaking `feat!:`, `chore(release): v1.37.0`, `docs(readme):`, plus subject+body+footer; 5 invalid: no type prefix, unknown `fixme:`, missing colon, empty description after `:`, >72 chars; 4 abort: empty / whitespace-only / comment-only / blank-prefix; 4 boundary: 72-char accept, 73-char reject, leading-whitespace trim, trailing-whitespace trim; 5 file-path / hook-presence). Live verification on this repo: `.git/hooks/commit-msg` rejected `git commit -m "broken"` with `type-prefix-missing` diagnostic, accepted `feat(setup): install commit-msg hook`, rejected a 94-char subject with `subject-too-long`. The M36 implementation commit (`feat(commits): adopt Conventional Commits v1.0.0`) and this ship commit (`chore(release): v1.37.0`) are the first two canonical CC commits on `main`. Out of scope (future FRs): auto-CHANGELOG generation from CC commit log; CI gate (GitHub Action) validating PR commits; CC-aware bump suggestion in `/ship-milestone`; M1–M35 history migration via `git filter-branch` (decisively rejected per /brainstorm 2026-04-27). (STE-133)

Total test count at release: 1071 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.

### Changed

- **STE-131 — README `## Workflow` diagram restructured with two-tier `classDef` styling, and orchestration prose rewritten to factually match `skills/implement/SKILL.md`.** Mermaid block declares two `classDef` rules: `spine` (stadium shape via `id(["/skill"])` syntax + green-tinted fill `#e1f5e1`, dark-green stroke `#2e7d32` at `stroke-width:3px`, black text — readable in both GitHub light and dark themes) and `secondary` (plain rectangle via `id["/skill"]` syntax + neutral-grey fill `#f5f5f5`, muted stroke `#999` at `stroke-width:1px`, dark-grey `#555` text). Five spine skills (`/setup`, `/brainstorm`, `/spec-write`, `/implement`, `/ship-milestone`) get the stadium shape + `:::spine`; nine secondary skills (`/tdd`, `/gate-check`, `/debug`, `/visual-check`, `/simplify`, `/spec-review`, `/spec-archive`, `/docs`, `/pr`) keep the plain rectangle + `:::secondary`. Approach 2 (phased subgraphs) per /brainstorm decision 2026-04-27; Approach 1 (linear flowchart with optional branches) and Approach 3 (two-lane specs↔code) explicitly rejected on cluttered-iteration-loop and complexity grounds. Single-FR milestone. Empty `deletedFiles` ⇒ vacuous no-op. Test coverage: `tests/cleanup_plan_verify_lines.test.ts` (6 helper cases) + `tests/gate-check-plan-verify-line-validity.test.ts` (7 probe cases including repo-self-check). (STE-126)

### Added

- **STE-121 — `buildFRFrontmatter` helper + `/spec-write` post-write probe-13 self-check.** New `adapters/_shared/src/fr_frontmatter.ts` exports `buildFRFrontmatter(spec, trackerBinding?)` returning canonical YAML between `---` delimiters with two branches (`mode: none` → `id: fr_<26-char ULID>` block, no `tracker:`; tracker mode → no `id:`, compact `tracker:\n  <key>: <id>` block). Mode/binding mismatch surfaces as `InvalidFrontmatterInputError`; the verbose `{ key, id, url }` shape surfaces as `InvalidTrackerShapeError` (NFR-10 canonical refusal citing STE-110 AC-STE-110.2). YAML-scalar escaping uses `JSON.stringify` only when titles carry `"` / `\` / `:` / `#` / leading whitespace — em-dash and other non-ASCII printables round-trip byte-identically. Companion `runFrontmatterShapeCheck(projectRoot, frFilePath)` re-runs probe-13's `runIdentityModeConditionalProbe` against the just-written file and throws `FRFrontmatterShapeError` (NFR-10 canonical) when violations surface. `/spec-write` SKILL.md §0b now mandates the helper at item 2 ("never author YAML by hand") and runs the post-write self-check at item 5 immediately after `Provider.sync(spec)` returns. One-time dry-run migration script at `scripts/migrate-fr-frontmatter-strip-id.ts` walks active tracker-mode FR files (excluding `archive/` per STE-22) and emits a unified diff stripping `id:` lines that survived the M29 STE-110 prose flip; pattern mirrors STE-114's `migrate-task-tracking-canonical.ts`. (STE-121)
- **STE-122 — `scanGuessedTrackerIdLiterals` post-write scanner + requirements template `AC-<tracker-id>.<N>` placeholders.** New `adapters/_shared/src/guessed_tracker_id_scan.ts` exports `scanGuessedTrackerIdLiterals(files)` returning `GuessedTrackerIdViolation[]` for any literal `\bAC-\d+\.\d+\b` token outside fenced / 4-space-indented / inline-backtick spans. The regex's `\d+` requirement excludes both canonical shapes — `AC-STE-1.1` (tracker-mode, letter-prefixed) and `AC-VDTAF4.1` (mode-none, alphanumeric short-ULID) — so the scanner only catches the bare-digit-milestone-numbered pre-substitution placeholder shape. `templates/spec-templates/requirements.md.template` flips per-FR ACs (lines 32–43) and traceability matrix rows (lines 78–79) from literal `AC-1.<N>` / `AC-2.<N>` to `AC-<tracker-id>.<N>`, mirroring STE-66's filename convention; the top-of-file comment block gains an explicit AC-IDs bullet referencing STE-50 (AC-prefix derivation), STE-66 (filename placeholder), and STE-122 (this AC). `/spec-write` SKILL.md §0b item 3 now carries the "Never emit literal `AC-<digit>.<N>` shape" rule, and item 5 runs the scanner against `[frFile, specs/requirements.md]` before /spec-write returns clean. Inline-backtick spans are stripped with space-padding so column positions remain accurate for any bare match later on the same line. (STE-122)
- **STE-123 — `/setup` step 8a audit-section post-condition + `synthesizeAuditSection` helper.** New `adapters/_shared/src/setup/synthesize_audit.ts` exports `synthesizeAuditSection(claudeMdPath, resolvedDefaults)` — deterministically writes one `## /setup audit` bullet per default-applied outcome (`branch_template` from step 7c plus the three `## Docs` flags from step 7d) using `appendAuditEntry` so output is byte-identical to per-step append output. Idempotent via `(step, field)` dedup keys parsed from existing entries; partial-section + complete-section + section-absent fixtures all green. Empty resolved-defaults table surfaces `AuditPostconditionUnsatisfiable` (NFR-10 canonical refusal) — invariant violation when CLAUDE.md shows default-applied outcomes but /setup's in-memory map is empty; aborts before step 8b's bootstrap commit lands. `hasDefaultApplicableOutcomes` is now exported from `setup_audit_section_presence.ts` for cross-module reuse — single source of truth between probe-19 at gate time and step 8a at /setup time. New `/setup` SKILL.md §8a sits between 7d (docs modes) and 8b (bootstrap commit), runs unconditionally regardless of prompt mode; vacuous on fully-interactive runs (`hasDefaultApplicableOutcomes` returns false). Option-5 fixture (smoke-test 2026-04-27 reproducer: pre-existing CLAUDE.md merged with defaults, no toolkit marker yet) confirms post-step-8a state satisfies probe-19 byte-identically. (STE-123)

## [1.33.0] — 2026-04-27 — "Guardrails"

M31 converts three discretionary checks (memory rules that only helped the current session) into hard gates that survive across LLM sessions and users. All three failure modes were surfaced during M30 spec-write 2026-04-27: tickets created without `project` landed outside the user's expected board (silent landing trap), no Linear `projectMilestone` was attached so milestone-side aggregation broke, and the LLM picked an already-shipped `M28` after a truncated `ls` of the archive. Three FRs, three new `/gate-check` probes, two new shared helpers, one widened adapter contract, one migration script. Test count: 861 → 937 (+76).

### Added

- **STE-117 — Tracker workspace binding (`### Linear` / `### Jira` Schema L sub-sections + adapter contract widening).** New canonical sub-sections under `## Task Tracking` carry workspace identity: `### Linear` requires `team:` + `project:` (optional `default_labels:`); `### Jira` requires `project:` (optional `default_labels:`). Parser is greedy until the next `##` or `###` heading; values are opaque UTF-8 (em-dash byte-preserved). New shared helper `readWorkspaceBinding(claudeMdPath, "linear" | "jira")` at `adapters/_shared/src/workspace_binding.ts` returns `{ team?, project?, defaultLabels? }` with vacuous-on-mode-none. `UpsertMetadataInput` widens with `team?` + `project?` (back-compat optional in the canonical TS surface; per-adapter required-on-create rules: Linear rejects creates without `project` per the silent-landing trap, Jira rejects creates without `project` per the Jira API requirement). `/setup` step 7b.6 prompts via `mcp__linear__list_teams` + `mcp__linear__list_projects --team <selected>` (live probe — no typed-from-memory) or Jira project key. `/spec-write` and `/implement` thread the values into every tracker create. New `/gate-check` probe #25 `task-tracking-workspace-binding-present` hard-fails tracker mode without a populated sub-section (vacuous on mode-none and on custom adapters). One-time migration script `scripts/migrate-task-tracking-add-workspace.ts` (dry-run only; emits unified diff to stdout for `patch -p1`). Dogfood: this repo's `CLAUDE.md` carries `### Linear` with `team: STE` + `project: DPT — Dev Process Toolkit`. (STE-117)
- **STE-118 — Auto-attach Linear project milestone in `/spec-write` + `/implement`.** New shared helper `attachProjectMilestone(provider, project, milestoneName, ticketId)` at `adapters/_shared/src/attach_project_milestone.ts` runs list → find-or-create → attach → verify-round-trip; mismatch raises `MilestoneAttachmentError` (NFR-10 canonical shape) so a silently-dropped Linear param never goes unnoticed. Idempotent on re-attach. Companion `planFileHeadingToMilestoneName(planFilePath)` strips the optional `{#M<N>}` anchor and preserves em-dash byte-for-byte (matching the M27 round-trip precedent). `/spec-write` invokes after `Provider.sync(spec)` returns the freshly-allocated tracker ID; `/implement` Phase 1 step 0.f invokes after the claim verification (idempotent, vacuous on archived FRs and `mode: none`). New `/gate-check` probe #26 `tracker-project-milestone-attached` (deps-injected `getIssue`) asserts `projectMilestone.name` byte-equals the canonical local heading; missing or mismatched binding hard-fails with both names rendered (em-dash drift visible) plus a remedy pointing at the `--rename-milestone M<N>` escape hatch. Vacuous on mode-none, archived FRs, FRs without a tracker block, and FRs whose plan file is missing (probe #27 owns that). M30 backfill verified: STE-115 + STE-116 carry `projectMilestone: "M30 — Stale doc references"` (Linear milestone object id `a890fdb0-0b5e-4683-9cdc-21d2f71b5fe5`). (STE-118)
- **STE-119 — Pre-allocation milestone-number guard + collision probe.** New mode-agnostic shared helper `nextFreeMilestoneNumber(specsDir, changelogPath?)` at `adapters/_shared/src/next_free_milestone_number.ts` runs a three-way scan (active `specs/plan/M<N>.md`, archived `specs/plan/archive/M<N>.md`, CHANGELOG `M<N>` references) and returns `{ next: max(union)+1, sources: { active, archived, changelog } }`. Gap-preserving (`max+1`, never reuses gap numbers). CHANGELOG scan is best-effort: missing / empty / no-M-references all return `[]` cleanly. `/spec-write` invokes before claiming any new `M<N>`; refuses with NFR-10 canonical shape (showing all three source breakdowns and the proposed next-free number) when the user explicitly types a taken `M<N>`. New `/gate-check` probe #27 `frontmatter-milestone-not-archived` walks every active FR and hard-fails three kinds of drift: (a) collision — active FR's `milestone:` points at an archived plan file (the post-edit catch for the M28 partial-`ls` bug), (b) orphan — milestone matches no plan file at all, (c) malformed — `milestone:` frontmatter missing entirely. Archived FRs and FRs whose milestone matches an active plan file pass. Mode-agnostic. (STE-119)

### Changed

- **Adapter contract: `upsert_ticket_metadata` widened.** `docs/tracker-adapters.md` Operations table grows `team?` / `project?` columns with the per-adapter required-on-create rules and an "Adapter authors" callout instructing out-of-tree adapters to forward both fields even when their tracker has no equivalent concept (silently dropping them masks failed bindings later). `adapters/linear.md` `upsert_ticket_metadata` row + Operations section detail the new flow: on create, both fields are resolved from call argument or `### Linear` sub-section, and the call is rejected with NFR-10 canonical shape if neither source supplies a value; on update (existing `id`), neither is forwarded (Linear cannot reassign team/project on an existing issue without explicit operator intent). `adapters/jira.md` documents `project` required-on-create per the Jira API requirement and notes `team` is silently dropped if forwarded. (STE-117)
- **`docs/patterns.md` § Schema L gains a "Workspace binding sub-sections" subsection** codifying the closed key set, parser rule, vacuous-on-mode-none semantics, and em-dash UTF-8 invariant. Migration helper pointer added. (STE-117)
- **`/gate-check` probe inventory grows by three.** Probes #25 / #26 / #27 registered with full row metadata and corresponding test files (`tests/gate-check-task-tracking-workspace-binding-present.test.ts`, `tests/gate-check-tracker-project-milestone-attached.test.ts`, `tests/gate-check-frontmatter-milestone-not-archived.test.ts`) per the STE-82 probe-authoring contract. (STE-117 / STE-118 / STE-119)

Total test count at release: 937 tests, 0 failures, 0 errors.
